The Terror of Zhènwǔ State 69

Japanese Ministry of Interior Strives to Suppress It

Police Armed Starting Next Year

Universal News, Tokyo: The Japanese Ministry of Interior, in view of the frequent occurrence of domestic violent acts since the May 15th Incident, with recent bank robbery incidents, is actively devising countermeasures. Measures already implemented include thorough security of seaports and plans to control firearms and gunpowder. In addition, it recognizes that the group action and armament of police officers is necessary to combat violence. It has been decided to establish a new special police force system starting next year, first in the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department, and then gradually emulate it in Osaka, Kyoto, Hyogo, Yokohama, and other major cities. The total personnel of the special police force established in the Tokyo Metropolitan Police Department will be 500, purely adopting a military style. Two hundred and seventy personnel will form one large unit, while the other two hundred and thirty personnel will be stationed at the Prime Minister's residence, various ministerial residences, and other important government offices to provide security in case of emergencies. Each large unit will be divided into three medium units, each medium unit with ninety people, and each medium unit divided into three small units, each small unit with thirty people. Each large unit will have a commander and deputy commander, and all members will be armed, receive military training, and be equipped with handguns, bulletproof vests, and other equipment.

British House of Commons Passes Ottawa Agreement 70

Liberal Party Launches Strong Criticism

Simon Defends the Government

Reuters, London, 20th: The parliamentary debate on the Ottawa Agreement entered its third day. Generally, supporters of free trade launched strong criticisms, while Foreign Secretary Simon defended the government. Opposition member Samuel claimed that the government's act of forcibly binding Parliament for more than a year during negotiations on tariff agreements was a violation of the constitution. Foreign Secretary Simon replied that this was not a new initiative and cited previous instances where Parliament was bound on tax rates for more than a year to prove his point. He also stated that the notion that Britain cannot successfully negotiate with other countries because of the Ottawa Agreement is inaccurate. Currently, various countries are contacting the British Foreign Office to negotiate trade matters, and Britain now has a tool to discuss with other countries. The Ottawa Agreement was passed with 451 votes in favor and 84 against.

Reuters, London, 21st: During the debate in the House of Commons tonight, British Foreign Secretary Simon explained the attitude of the Liberal Party in remaining in the cabinet, citing the words of Gladstone and Cobden, asking his former comrades to consider the serious situation in the face of many problems currently encountered by the country, and then decide whether to attack the current government. Havas News Agency, London, 20th: Britain will soon conduct negotiations on tariff matters with certain countries, and the result may be to increase the current British import tariff rate. This move is highly possible because after Britain concluded the Ottawa Agreement, it agreed to grant the minimum preferential tax rate to each dominion. However, for other countries outside the empire, the general tariff rules are uniformly applied. Therefore, if Britain wants to favor certain countries, it must increase the tax rate applicable to other countries. Accordingly, there will be three types of British import tariff rates: (1) The tariff rate applicable to all imperial possessions. (2) The intermediate tariff rate, i.e., the current external tariff rate, exclusively enjoyed by favored countries. (3) The tariff rate applicable to other foreign countries, which is higher than the current external tariff rate.

Various Sectors in Britain Promote Disarmament Efforts 71

Prime Minister MacDonald Will Visit Geneva

Seeking a Turnaround on the Disarmament Issue

Reuters, London, 20th: When Prime Minister MacDonald met with a delegation visiting the Foreign Office today to discuss disarmament, he mentioned that he and Foreign Secretary Simon may visit Geneva to achieve a better understanding among the various countries. Among the delegation were leaders from various churches, who strongly urged that the work of the disarmament conference be accelerated. Archbishop of Canterbury Lang delivered a speech, saying that they hoped for a strict ban on tanks, artillery, submarines, military aircraft, and warships over 10,000 tons, and asked that Britain cooperate very closely with the United States in disarmament efforts. Foreign Secretary Simon, who was also present, replied with the same words as the Archbishop, and recalled that a "qualitative" disarmament was actually initiated by the British delegation to the disarmament conference. Prime Minister MacDonald then delivered a speech, saying that the understanding between Britain and the United States regarding disarmament cannot be broken without a major spiritual change. The two countries are now trying to create a similar situation in Europe. He welcomes the moral pressure placed on disarmament, but advocates of peace must not only think from a moral perspective, but also clearly understand other possibilities in the overall situation.

Four-Power Conference Plan Fails 72

National News Agency, Paris, 20th: News from London: The plan for a four-power disarmament preparatory conference is now considered to have been practically shelved. Currently, the British government is considering two options: one is a conference of France, Italy, and Britain to consider Germany's demands for equality; the other is to continue the disarmament conference as before, proceeding with theories close to those of Germany, even if Germany does not join. Although the second option, especially continuing the disarmament conference, seems to be more agreeable to the French government, it is heard that the British government still advocates holding a three-power conference and making concessions to Germany, with only certain reservations attached. Furthermore, French newspapers revealed today that during a meeting of the Foreign Affairs Committee on Wednesday, Herriot, in response to questions from members, expressed that in the event that Germany unilaterally abolished the disarmament clauses of the Treaty of Versailles and expanded its military, France has no intention of using force, but will submit the matter to the International Court of Justice for public judgment, and explained the reasons why France previously insisted on Germany paying the final installment of reparations at the Lausanne Conference, due to pressure from the United States on the old Allied powers. According to Herriot's words, it has caused shock to the world and is expected to cause extremely important repercussions.

You Drive a Car While I Am Still Hungry 76

A Cry of Sorrow from British Unemployed

Reuters, London, 20th: Prince George of Britain drove to the west end of London last night, planning to attend the completion ceremony of the Seafarers' Rest at Poplar. When Prince George arrived at the place, some people shouted, "You have a car while I have no food!" But this cry was soon drowned out by general cheers. Before the prince arrived, many unemployed people crowded into the new building but were driven out by the police, and three people were arrested.

Public Telegram 77

Telegram from Xining: All newspaper offices are hereby informed that the Qilian Yushu area of Hainan is the throat of Qinghai and Kangding and the shield of the Southwest. Since March of this year, Tibetan troops have been rampant, taking advantage of the weakness of our Yushu defense forces to break into the border, occupy our territory, massacre our people, and commit arson, murder, and looting to the extreme. Their behavior is completely inhumane. Bu Fang believes that the Tibetan side is also one of the five major ethnic groups and wants to treat them peacefully, unwilling to resort to arms. Therefore, he requested the Qinghai Provincial Government to send personnel to appease them, hoping they would realize their mistakes, withdraw their troops, and seek a return to their old harmony. However, the Tibetan troops, led by Wang Qianbu, relied on their backers, were obsessed with aggression, and not only refused to listen to reason, but also mobilized heavy troops and launched the first attack, besieging Jiegou for several months. The defenders of Jiegou, led by Ma Zai and Ma Biao, were outnumbered and weak, but still hoped for peace, ultimately adopting a defensive posture. When there was no hope for peace and supplies and ammunition were exhausted, they were forced to resist. For national defense and for the sake of the people, Bu Fang believed that losing Yushu would endanger Qinghai, and if Qinghai was in turmoil, then half of the Northwest would also be in unrest. Therefore, he dispatched his troops, including Regimental Commander Lu and Brigade Commander Ma, to successively depart to aid Yushu. The officers and soldiers did not shy away from the thousands of miles of miasma-filled wilderness, and after making efforts to break the enemy's siege of Jiegou, they restored all the lost territories of La Xiu, Da Xiao Su Mang, and Ang Qian in the shortest possible time. Taking advantage of the victory, they advanced to attack the Dangtouke and other temples under the jurisdiction of Kangding. The enemy concentrated on important locations, and then attacked Zhengke. They are currently moving to assist the Sichuan army in crossing the river to jointly attack Changdu. If the borders of Kangding are completely restored, a telegram will be sent to the central government for instructions. Bu Fang hopes that the Dalai Lama will awaken, approve the restoration of the land and sovereignty of the Panchen Lama, and that both sides will reaffirm their old friendship, remain as citizens of the party and country forever, and consolidate the border of Jiangbei as securely as a rock. This is what Bu Fang silently prays for day and night. I respectfully present the details of the recapture of the lost territories of Hainan and the military details of the planned joint capture of Changdu by telegram to the entire country to clarify the truth, and I hope to receive instructions so that I can follow them. Commander Ma Bufang of the Southern Qinghai Border Defense Garrison bows and signs.

Future Record of the Japan-U.S. Naval War (Continued) 78

General Pollard, a hawkish admiral, is a scholar of war theory. During World War I, he created his own unique strategy. His tactics were instructed by the German military strategist General Graf Schlieffen, who studied the [Five-Percent Advantage Ratio N-Squared Method] of warfare. The mathematical basis of his warfare, researched by Japanese scholar Dr. Nomura, is explained as follows:

If Army A is N1 and Army B is N2, and the two armies engage in combat, then the defeat time of N2 can be calculated.

According to this calculation method, after the first salvo of a 60% navy, it can be completely annihilated in 27 minutes. Therefore, in the Washington and London Conferences, the ratio of Japan's navy being 6 and the United States' navy being 10 was stipulated. This is the implication of the logical strategist General Pollard, who confuses strategy with the mathematical formula of the N-squared method. He believes that with an advantage rate of 67%, he can definitely defeat Japan. Now, Pollard wants to implement a creative strategy to force the Japanese navy to be 60%, so the London Naval Treaty can be renamed the Pollard Treaty. The aforementioned ["Wheel Formation"] is the application of [the formula of the N-squared method to the fleet's ocean-crossing method. However, the U.S. Navy is most afraid of this formation, which is [the method of preserving the fighting power of battleships] in the event of a surprise attack en route by the Japanese submarine fleet. Originally, the fleet sequence during ocean-crossing operations, including the combined supply units, would reach 30 nautical miles or more. In order to counter a surprise attack by the enemy fleet in this sequence, we must deploy a search column. However, the distance of this column 200 nautical miles ahead of the U.S. fleet, the distance of the search column team is a maximum of 25 nautical miles in terms of visibility. We use ten frontline cruisers, and even at night, due to the narrow field of vision, we have to deploy a double search column, so we place another eight cruisers in the second search column. However, the enemy, with a superior cruiser fleet, will definitely attempt to destroy a part of our Japanese search column, or the enemy will infiltrate submarines to attack our main fleet. At this time, we can use light cruisers to defend against it. In 1928, General Hughes explained the wheel formation at the Senate Naval Committee and requested a budget for building warships. In 1930, Admiral Pollard supplemented Hughes's opinion, planning to deploy 8-inch gun cruisers in the search column and use 6-inch gun cruisers in the wheel formation. According to this plan, the United States is confident that it can win the battle in the Pacific. Although the Japanese navy has a defensive plan in terms of war objectives and military strength, we consider this wheel formation to be extremely dangerous. Why? According to the views of naval strategists, the wheel formation is originally a cautious defensive formation. If it points its cannons at us and moves out of the Hawaiian base, it will fall into the operating range of the Japanese navy. At that time, the sea area hundreds of nautical miles east of 囗囗囗 Island and 囗囗 coast will be an extremely dangerous area for the U.S. Navy, and the movement of Japanese submarines, the deployment of mines, the activity of surprise attack forces, and the progress of the Japanese main fleet will be difficult to understand, and the direction of progress will be unclear. Then the U.S. Navy will definitely feel greatly confused. Recalling the World War, Admiral Jellicoe of Britain led a fleet twenty times superior to that of Beatty's, but during the Battle of Jutland, he was deeply afraid of a night attack by German submarines. Moreover, the actual numbers of the Japanese and U.S. navies are not much different. The U.S. Navy's expedition of more than 3,000 nautical miles, after several days and nights of waves on the ocean, is mentally exhausted, and the instability of its combat power is conceivable. From this point of view, although the U.S. Navy has an attacking force, it has to take a defensive posture in the Western Pacific theater. This so-called wheel formation is actually a formation destined for defeat. (To be continued)

Chiang Restrains the Sichuan War 79

Rumored to Have Summoned Representatives from Both Liu Factions to Inquire About Sichuan Matters

Both Sides Engage in Main Force Contact in Eastern Sichuan

Correspondence from Hankou: The conflict between the two Liu factions in Sichuan Province has been brewing for a long time. Both sides are poised and ready for a decisive battle. For the past half-month, the situation has been getting more serious day by day. After unofficial contact between the two sides, a real battle by the main forces is taking place. This time the conflict between the two armies initially took place in the Shunqing, Wusheng, and Liemianxi areas. Then the 24th Army of Liu Wenhui concentrated in Zizhong and Neijiang, with Zhang Zhihe, commander of the 1st Division, as the commander of the southern route, Chen Hongwen, commander of the 2nd Division, as the commander of the northern route, and Xia Zhongshi, commander of the 3rd Division, as the commander of the central route. The 21st Army of Liu Xiang concentrated in the eastern Sichuan area, with Tang Shizun, commander of the 1st Division, as the commander of the central route, Wang Zuanxu, commander of the 2nd Division, as the commander of the northern route, and Pan Wenhua, commander of the Training Division, as the commander of the southern route. And the matter has become more extensive. Liu Wenhui has also withdrawn the Xikang defense army, and Liu Xiang has also withdrawn the troops suppressing bandits in Hubei to increase the strength of the fighting force. Although both sides are still trying their best to deny this, the troops of Guo Xun stationed in Hubei have indeed returned to Sichuan, and the office of the commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River stationed in western Hubei has also been uniformly abolished, which can no longer be concealed. Once the deployments of both sides are completed, contact will be made. It is reported that Luo Zezhou's troops suffered a slight setback. The center of the battle has moved from the Shunqing area to places such as Chuanjin and Yongchuan. According to reports from Sichuan, the front teams of both sides have indeed made contact, and the main battle is about to begin. It is still difficult to predict how far it will expand in the future. In summary, the outbreak of this war can be divided into seven periods: the first is the preparation period for both sides, which was long before a month ago. Both sides did not admit to preparing for war. The second is the period of mutual attacks, which was at the end of last month and the beginning of this month. Both sides reported to the government, each claiming to be the troublemaker. The third is the period of central restraint, and both sides expressed their compliance, and said that even if the conflict started by others, they would not return a single shot. The fourth is the period of provocation by both sides, that is, contact in places such as Shunqing and Wusheng, which was in the early part of this month. Both sides have fought preliminary battles. The fifth is the period of proposals by second-level generals, with the second-level generals proposing a plan to resolve the Sichuan situation through the Suining Conference. The sixth is the period of the central government sending senior officials, but since no one is willing to take on this important task, they have not yet been assigned. The seventh is the recent period of the outbreak of the great war, and the Sichuan situation has become even more difficult to handle. Chiang Kai-shek, chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, is paying close attention to the internal strife in Sichuan Province and has strictly ordered both sides to avoid conflict, and has said "Taking care of the Sichuan situation is the way to maintain the country." Currently, due to the tense situation, it is reported that at 5:00 PM on the 20th, he summoned Wu Jinhang, representative of Liu Wenhui, and Qiu Jia, representative of Liu Xiang, at the Yihé Village residence to inquire about Sichuan matters, and also telegraphed Xu Zhongqi and others from the Sichuan Provincial Party Committee to come to Hankou to inquire about internal conditions in detail so as to resolve the Sichuan situation as soon as possible. According to the telegram from Xu and others, they have already taken the Yongnian ship eastward from Chongqing on the 19th and are expected to arrive in Hankou around tomorrow or the day after tomorrow. (October 20)

He Chengjun Goes to Yuekou to Supervise the Suppression of He Long and Kuang Jixun's Remnant Bandits 80

The Administrative Office Urges the Establishment of Yuekou, Advancing to the Front Lines When Necessary

Before Departing, He Pays Respects to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and Seeks Instructions

Hankou Correspondence: Kuang Jixun's remnant bandits, after suffering a disastrous defeat, were led by Xu Xiangqian and Cai Shenxi, dispersing and fleeing in different directions. Cai's bandits fled to Anhui province, where they were surrounded and suppressed by the troops of Shangguan Yunxiang and Hao Mengling, and the matter was expected to be resolved. However, the bandits led a large force, crossed the Pinghan Railway, and fled into the territory of Suixian County in northern Hubei, where they joined forces with He Long's remnant bandits. Although they were ambushed along the way by the Nationalist army and suffered heavy losses, their ambition to stage a comeback has not diminished. The local military authorities, in order to thoroughly eliminate the remnant bandits, have redeployed their forces, adopting a large-scale encirclement and suppression strategy. Heavy troops have been stationed in the areas of Pinghan City, Xiaogan, Huayuan, Guangshui, Wusheng Pass, and Xinyang, both to protect the railway and to threaten the bandits. In addition, the two divisions of Wei Lihuang's command, led by Zhuang Fusheng and Li Mo'an, as well as the 51st Division led by Fan Shisheng, the 44th Division led by Xiao Zhichu, the 41st Division led by Zhang Zhenhan, and the 34th Brigade led by Luo Qijiang, have been dispatched to encircle and suppress the bandits in different directions. Chiang, Li, and Xiao's three divisions have already arrived in Suixian County, Fan's division has arrived in Yicheng, Zhang's division has crossed the Xiang River and marched north from Jingzhong, and Luo's brigade is stationed on the border between Sui and Zao, simultaneously launching attacks on the remnant bandits. He Chengjun has also been ordered to go to supervise the troops. He returned to Hankou from southern Hubei, and his old illness relapsed. He has now recovered somewhat and has dispatched Yang Yadong, a senior staff officer of the Pacification Headquarters, staff officer Min Wenhui, secretary Li Peng, adjutant Wen Zhenshen, quartermaster Zhu Xiangwen, and a company of military police on the evening of the 19th, taking the Han Chuan and Jing Hua steamboats, to depart for Yuekou first, to organize the administrative office. On the morning of the 20th, at 9:00 AM, He went to Yihua Village to pay respects to Chiang Kai-shek, the chairman, to seek instructions. In the afternoon, at 2:30 PM, he went to Wangjiadun Airport, taking the No. 6 aviation team's transport plane, the Douglas, and flew to Yuekou. The plane returned to Hankou at 5:30 PM. According to reports, He arrived at Yuekou at 4:00 PM. It is heard that He's trip to Yuekou is to discuss with Xu Yuanquan the aftermath of the suppression in central Hubei. After a brief stay, he will go to the front lines to command. The administrative office will be temporarily located in Yuekou and will be moved to the front lines when necessary. According to He's words to visitors before his departure, he said, "A few days ago, I went to Longgang, originally planning to go to the counties of southern Hubei to inspect the local reconstruction and to discuss relief measures for the recovered bandit areas with Division Commander Guo Rudong. Later, I returned to Hankou for medical treatment due to illness, so I entrusted the pacification and suppression matters to Division Commander Guo, together with Commander Zhang Gang and Brigade Commander Li Dingwu, for proper handling. There are now no traces of bandits in southern Hubei, and the local area is very peaceful. Given some time, it will not be difficult to restore the original state. Now, because the recovered bandit areas in central Hubei urgently need relief, I am specially going to inspect and to discuss the aftermath with Army Commander Xu Yuanquan. As for Xu Xiangqian's bandit gang, after being severely suppressed by the Nationalist army in eastern Hubei, their strength is limited. After fleeing west, they were intercepted by Luo Qijiang's brigade. Although they attempted to join forces with He Long's bandits, they will find it difficult to survive. Now, Wei Lihuang, Xiao Zhichu, and Fan Shisheng's troops have separately pursued and blocked them. I will go to command when necessary. The remnant bandits are now surrounded on all sides, and it should not be difficult to annihilate them in one fell swoop." It is heard that He will stay for a while on this trip, and the date of his return has not yet been determined. (October 20th)

A Major Fire in Qingdao's Slums 81

Burning Over Three Hundred and Sixty Households

More Than Fifteen Hundred Victims

Qingdao Correspondence: In this city, fires occur almost every month, sometimes several or even dozens of times. However, most of the affected households are business firms, and eight or nine out of ten have fire insurance, so even if they encounter such accidents, they can still cope. Unexpectedly, last night (the 18th), at around 7:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in the slum of Xiling Dirty Ditch, burning over three hundred and sixty households. The victims are now sleeping in the streets, and more than fifteen hundred people have been rendered homeless. The tragedy is unprecedented and is truly a catastrophe. The circumstances of the fire and the relief measures are described below:

Location of the Fire: The area around Xiling Dirty Ditch is where the poor are concentrated, and the houses are all made of wood, making them highly susceptible to fires. A fire occurred there last spring, burning over two hundred households. Subsequently, the Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus, in order to prevent fires and improve the appearance of the city, ordered the residents to move out and demolish all the wooden houses to build affordable housing. However, the residents have repeatedly delayed and have not yet moved. Last night, at 6:30 PM, in the Hexing neighborhood on the west side of the area, a carpentry shop owned by a contractor surnamed Wang had a large amount of timber piled up. Due to the carelessness of a cook named Ning in preparing food, the wood chips and shavings caught fire. In addition, the weather has been dry and arid recently, and the fire quickly spread with the help of the wind, becoming uncontrollable. The wooden houses in the area are densely packed and connected end to end, making it very easy for the fire to spread. In an instant, the flames soared into the sky, but fortunately, it was still early, and men, women, and children were able to escape, avoiding being buried in the fire.

Relief Efforts: When the fire broke out, the North China Match Company in Dongzhen also accidentally caught fire at the same time, and the fire brigade had already rushed to put out that fire. It was not until 7:20 PM that the fire brigade returned, but by then the fire had already become raging and impossible to extinguish. As a result, all the wooden houses were reduced to ashes. The men, women, and children who escaped from the fire were scattered on the nearby roads, and the cries of women and children were unbearable to hear. Chu Zhen, the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, Yu Jinhe, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, and Sun Bingxian, the Director of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, all arrived at the scene to maintain order. The chiefs and police officers of the First and Second Branches also turned out in full force and made considerable efforts to maintain order in the fire zone and to rescue the victims. It was not until around 10:00 PM that the fire gradually subsided.

Damage Assessment: According to the post-incident investigation by the local district office, the area west of Guancheng Road is Dirty Ditch, which is divided into Guancheng Fifth Road. Starting from the corner of the cattle yard of the slaughterhouse company and heading south, Guancheng Second Road, from No. 30 to the intersection of Tengxian Road, extending to No. 270, a total of over three hundred and sixty households were destroyed, and more than fifteen hundred men, women, and children were rendered homeless and urgently need relief. Although the residents in the area are all poor, they have lived there for seven or eight years, and about half of them had household possessions worth four or five hundred yuan, but none of them had fire insurance.

Relief Arrangements: The Public Security and Social Affairs Bureaus, deeply sympathetic to the plight of the poor residents who have suffered such a tragedy, have jointly dispatched personnel to make arrangements for relief in the disaster area. Today, they have begun to register the number of affected households and are temporarily housing the victims in the cattle yard of the slaughterhouse company on Guancheng Road. The manager of the company has voluntarily donated 600 yuan, giving each person 4 jiao to maintain their current livelihood. Other relief issues will be handled after a thorough investigation. (October 19th)

Local Correspondence

Taicang 82

A General Reduction of 30% in Grain Tribute Throughout the County: This year's autumn harvest has been assessed, and the Director of the Finance Bureau has personally inspected the various townships in accordance with regulations. A meeting was held at the county government on the 18th, inviting local representatives to discuss and decide on a general reduction of 30.3% in the county's grain tribute, with an actual collection of 66.7%. The matter has been jointly submitted by the county government and the Finance Bureau to the provincial authorities for approval and implementation.

Villagers Riot to Protect Temple: The Shisi Security Corps of this county, due to a lack of funds, previously removed the chessboards in front of the Huchang Temple and converted them into telegraph poles. Forty temple trees and the surplus rent from the temple fields were allocated to the corps' expenses. Upon hearing this news, villagers gathered several hundred people the day before yesterday to protect the temple, demanding that the destroyed statues, chessboards, and temple trees be assessed and compensated. They first went to the home of Zhang Shushi, the head of the branch corps, but he was not there, so they went to the home of the secretary, Zhang Jiong, and destroyed his belongings. They then went to the homes of the corps leader, Yu Huimin, and Yang Lin, and set fire to their houses. The township chiefs, Lu Shouzhi and Wang Yangtian, and the temple directors, Yang Ziting, seeing the disaster they had caused, came forward to mediate. As a result, the Security Corps compensated Huchang Temple 130 yuan. The remaining judicial matters are being handled separately in court.

Wuxi 83

Telegrams Requesting the Lifting of the Rice Embargo and the Abolition of Excessive Taxes: The Shanghai Local Association, concerned that the low price of grain was affecting the rural economy, which has a significant impact on the entire society, specially dispatched representatives and invited commercial leaders from rice-producing counties in the interior of Jiangsu Province to hold a meeting in Wuxi on the 17th and 18th. They resolved to request the government to lift the ban on rice exports, impose import duties on foreign rice, abolish excessive taxes, and stop foreign wheat loans. Yesterday, Mu Ouchu and others, who were present at the meeting, jointly telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Industry, with the following original telegram: [In Shanghai and Jiangsu, due to the excessively low price of rice, farmers and merchants are in distress. The Shanghai Local Association has initiated a special invitation to local officials from various rice-producing counties in Jiangsu Province to hold a joint meeting in Wuxi County on the 17th and 18th of this month. After two days of lengthy discussions, the written proposals and the purpose of the meeting were summarized, and it was unanimously agreed that, speaking for Jiangsu, the rice embargo should be lifted as soon as possible. It should first be implemented in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to facilitate circulation, and the county governments and water and land police should be ordered to provide immediate and effective protection and should not cause any delays. It is also requested that the central government promptly implement import duties on foreign rice and issue orders to all provinces to abolish rice

permits and other excessive taxes that hinder domestic circulation. Regarding foreign wheat loans, it is hoped that the government will listen to public opinion, stop negotiations, and cancel the process. However, if there is any smuggling or covert transportation of rice abroad, strict prohibition and punishment should be enforced. The meeting's opinions were unanimous, and this special telegram is sent for your consideration and implementation. We are anxiously awaiting your instructions.]

Beef Merchants Petition for Lifting the Ban: Beef merchants from various counties such as Jiangsu Province, Wuxi Jin Wanxing, Yang Yongxing, and Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Changzhou, Suzhou, Kunshan, etc., jointly went to Nanjing's Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Ministry of Industry, Zhenjiang Provincial Party Headquarters, Provincial Government, Department of Industry, and Department of Civil Affairs, and other nine organizations, to submit documents to request the opening of the beef market, citing that the implementation of the ban was ineffective, that the slaughter of draft cattle had already exceeded the permitted limits and was rampant, harming agriculture, that Japanese enemies were taking advantage of the situation to purchase beef to supply their troops, endangering the nation and the people, and hindering the fundamental agricultural industry. They listed twelve methods to save the situation. It is now heard that the authorities have approved the slaughter of vegetable cattle and the prohibition of draft cattle in order to protect farmers and merchants.

Robbery at Anjia She: Cheng Yuanjia, a farmer near Anjia She in the Fourth District of Wuyi, was suddenly attacked the night before last by several armed robbers who broke into his house and ransacked it at will. Cheng Yuan and his wife were beaten, and all their clothing and cash were taken away.

Detainees Clash with Director: Zhao Fengxian, the newly appointed prison officer and warden of Wuyi, recently appointed Yang Jinlian as the director of the branch prison. After Yang arrived at the prison, for some unknown reason, he offended the detainees, resulting in a major conflict. The prisoners threw mud and sewage at Yang, drenching him from head to toe. Warden Zhao rushed to investigate and arrested the ringleaders, detaining them for further investigation.

Suppressing Bandits in Xinchang, Shengzhou, and Fenghua Counties: The three counties of Zhexin (Chang), Sheng (Zhou), and Feng (Hua) are adjacent to each other, and the territory is mountainous, with bandits appearing and disappearing unpredictably. Ningbo 90

Large Number of Refugees Passing Through Ningbo: A group of 111 refugees from Sixian County, Anhui Province, arrived at Zhenhai by boat from Shanghai the day before yesterday. Hefei 91

Leader of Merchant Corps Executed for Colluding with Bandits: In the area around Yuantuan Village in the northern countryside, bandits have been rampant in recent months. Because the leader of the merchant corps in that village, Yu Junchen, colluded with them, they carried guns in teahouses and restaurants during the day and formed gangs at night to commit murder and arson. The people repeatedly went to the county to file charges. Magistrate Wang negotiated with Ni Rongxian, the head of the Second Security Regiment, to send troops to surround and search the village. The bandits resisted fiercely. In addition to killing the bandit leaders Zhu Wuzang, Wang Xiaoba, Xiang Yikai, Wu Kefa, and Xiang Yizhi on the spot, they also captured 22 people, including the leader of the merchant corps, Yu Junchen, the bandits Wang Chengming and Liu Shitian, and Li Chengshi. After strict interrogation by Magistrate Wang, Yu admitted to colluding with and harboring bandits, Wang and Liu directly admitted to repeatedly committing robberies, and Li Chengshi directly admitted to being a bandit. All were sentenced to death. On the 16th, the four prisoners were paraded through the streets and then taken to Caidatang for execution by firing squad.

Letter

Letter from the 19th Route Army Office in Nanjing 92

Sir, I am writing to you regarding the report (Nanjing telegram) in your newspaper on the 14th, which stated that the person in charge of our office said that the Fujian Provincial Defense Army was plotting to resist our army and that the newly formed Second Division, led by Lu Xingbang, was also planning to join the Provincial Defense Army. This news is completely false. The person in charge of our office did not make such statements, and the Fujian Provincial Defense Army and the newly formed Second Division have not joined forces to resist our army. We are concerned that people outside may misunderstand the truth, so we are specially requesting that your newspaper correct this matter as soon as possible. Thank you for your attention. 19th Route Army Office in Nanjing, October 19th.

(Educational News) (Important News)

Luo Jialun, President of National Central University, Gives a Lecture 93

Forming an Organic National Culture

(Part 3)

Speaking of an organic national culture, we must especially mention its most important aspect: first, everyone must have a shared awareness of revitalizing the Chinese nation. Today, we have reached a crossroads of life and death. If we are content to perish from this point, there is nothing to say. Otherwise, we must strive hard, seek life from death, and revitalize our nation. Each of us should strive under this shared awareness. Second, we must ensure that the efforts of all parts of the culture become coordinated with each other under this shared awareness. If the various parts cannot be coordinated, they will inevitably become scattered and unsystematic, leading to mutual conflicts and negating all the forces. Therefore, whether studying literature, science, engineering, agriculture, law, or education, all should be properly coordinated, with a consistent spirit and orderly steps, to move towards the common goal of establishing a national culture. Schools have been established in China for many years, but the results have been scattered and disordered due to improper allocation, especially because there is no shared national awareness to dominate them, so various efforts do not cooperate with each other. As a result, they not only fail to achieve the effect of cooperation and progress but also criticize each other and achieve nothing. Now, the number of university professors and students in the country is already limited. If they cannot work together towards the goal of building a national culture, it is a great loss to the nation. If this continues, it will inevitably reduce and even eliminate the vitality of the nation. People scold us for being an unorganized country, and we should be pained by this. But what we feel is not only political disorganization but also the disorganization of the entire society, especially the disorganization of culture. In the future, if we want to make China an organized country, we must quickly create an organized national culture, that is, an organic national culture. I used the historical facts of Germany above to illustrate the importance of our mission, but it is not to ask everyone to learn the so-called Prussianism but to emulate their efforts to create an independent national spirit from culture.

If we want to bear the aforementioned mission, we must cultivate a new style of learning. Whether president, faculty, or students, we must strive to shift the atmosphere, from the atmosphere of one school to the atmosphere of the entire country. Administrative affairs cannot be abandoned, but we run schools not just for administrative affairs, not to do things without a purpose. If we only talk about administration, it is best to ask foreign firms and compradors to run the university. We must have lofty ideals as goals of effort, believing that the success of ideals is greater than the success of anyone. Any personal sacrifice is worthwhile for the sake of ideals. I believe that if a new style of learning can be cultivated, our mission can be achieved.

Achievements of the Special Contracted Farmland in Xinxun Village, Wuxian County 94

The Wuxian County Shanzhen Bridge Rural Improvement Association has been managing the cooperative rice paddies and specially contracted farmlands near the association. Davidson's First Lecture on Football Refereeing 108

Responsibilities and Powers of Football Referees (Continued)

The referee cannot condone tolerance

I will now tell you one sentence in the competition rules that referees must pay close attention to, which is [The referee cannot condone tolerance in his work], and there is nothing more related to the referee or extremely difficult than this sentence. If the referee actually carries out condoning tolerance, then the audience, players, staff, etc. will regard the referee as either weak and incompetent, or completely incomprehensible to the game. Sometimes, because of condoning, unwilling to implement Article 9 and Article 17 (according to the penalty for a twelve-yard kick), unknowingly, a bad impression occurs, that is, the referee gives one party convenience, and the other party does not have it, or one player is penalized with a twelve-yard kick, and the other party's player commits it, then he is tolerated.

Once a decision is made, it must be upheld

One more important point, I would like to bring to your attention, is that a referee must have a faithful and impartial judgment. Once a judgment has been made, even if the sky is about to fall, it must be upheld, and it must never be changed. Do not make a mistake in one judgment, and then try to make it average, and give the other party a favorable judgment. Players can forgive one mistake, but if this method is adopted to average the mistake, then the referee's trust will be completely lost from now on. Who is without fault? I also dare not say that there are no mistakes on the field, and not subject to criticism. It is more necessary to determine the handling of the game based on the referee's own observations and opinions, and never to handle it based on the opinions of observers, players, or staff.

Once decided, uphold it

Enforcing a referee has no distinction in rank

There is no distinction in rank in executing a referee, although there may be different standards, each referee's responsibility is to implement the rules of the game with a courageous and fair spirit. There should be no distinction in rank in executing a referee or handling a competition. The rules of the game are equally applied to any competition, such as letting go of one player who fouls, and punishing other players who foul, which is unfair. Furthermore, it is not possible to relax responsibility in the first half and tighten it in the second half. The implementation of the rules of the game cannot be tight on one person and loose on another. It is equally powerful to implement it on any team, and the referee's first responsibility is to treat any team under the rule of law in an impartial manner.

The "Impossibilities" of a Scottish Referee 109

Here is an introduction to the [Referee's Impossibilities] in the Scottish Referee's Manual: (1) Do not make the team wait for you, you must arrive on time; (2) Do not be impatient, be calm; (3) Do not instruct players on the field, you are the interpreter of the rules; (4) Do not change the decision afterwards to make it suitable for everything; (5) Do not value the audience, you can ignore them and make your will your will; (6) Do not refuse a polite request to explain a judgment, answer humbly, you can gain the trust of the players; (7)

Finally, do not forget the advanced referees in the training institute, they all rely on your protection and improvement.

No need to worry about newspaper coverage

There is no need to worry about newspaper reports. In my experience, very few newspaper reporters know the rules of the game in detail. Do not be elated by newspaper praise, and do not be discouraged by criticism. If sometimes it is appropriate for you to be diminished, you cannot maintain the same high standard, disappointing people, and therefore not praised as before for your handling.

Davidson's great delight

To conclude my words, my greatest delight in executing a referee is that when I look back at the Scottish competition fields of the previous session, I am honored and delighted that I have done my best to become an honorable referee. On the day I left Scotland, I told my colleagues this, I feel that I can hold my head high and leave the field without blushing, confident that I can live up to the name of a referee. I deeply hope to continue to maintain this spirit forever, and then when I put down the silver whistle, I can also say this and talk about my refereeing situation in Shanghai.

(New Basketball Techniques (16) (No Reprinting) Originally Written by Claire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yiqin) 112

This formation contains close passes, twists, blocking opponents, and dribbling to shoot, giving the opposing team a difficult-to-defend offensive method. This method was passed on to Pierce Works, who used to teach Bruins at the University of California in Los Angeles. It is recorded below:

Number 2 and number 3 each run forward. Number 2 receives the close pass from number 1 and immediately passes it to number 3. Number 5 runs out of the corner at the same time, and number 4 also runs from under the basket to the corner. Number 3 is open. Number 3 immediately turns around and passes the ball to number 5. When turning around, he also takes advantage of the momentum to block the guard of number 5. Number 5 should dribble straight to the basket while unguarded.

Heads of Various Ministries Gather in Shanghai 113

Wang Leaves the Country with German Doctor This Afternoon

Zhang Fakui and Eight Others Accompany Him

Zeng Zhongming Only Sees Him Off to Hong Kong

Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, is scheduled to leave Shanghai this afternoon on the French mail ship André Lebon to recuperate in Germany. Wang's wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, her daughter, Dr. Knoll, secretaries, and attendants will all accompany him, a total of nine people. The heads of various ministries of the Executive Yuan all came to Shanghai yesterday morning to bid farewell to Wang. Chiang's representative, Zhang Qun, and Yan's representative, Zhao Pilian, also visited Wang yesterday morning to see him off. Wang also issued a statement last night, expressing his views on the Sichuan-Shandong conflict. The details are described separately below.

Ministers Arrive in Shanghai 114

In addition to a few who had arrived in Shanghai earlier, the heads of various ministries of the Executive Yuan, including Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wengan, Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin, Chief of Staff Zhu Peide, Secretary-General of the Central Standing Committee Ye Chucang, Secretary-General of the Central Political Council Tang Youren, Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, Director of the Department of Health Liu Hengrui, and Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Shi Qingyang, successively arrived in Shanghai around 8:00 AM yesterday morning. Song Ziwen visits Wang at Chu's residence (Photo by Li Zunyong)

He Yingqin's Speech 117

Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin told reporters yesterday that the dispute between the two Lius in Sichuan has been stopped by the central government with a telegram. No personnel will be sent to Sichuan for the time being. In Shandong, Han has complied with the order to withdraw his troops and is awaiting the central government's disposal. Han's troops will retreat to the west of Weixian, and the five counties of Laiyang will be designated as Liu Shi's garrison. This is indeed the case. The opening date of the Third Plenary Session has been tentatively set for December 1st or 15th, and is awaiting final decision.

Meeting with Representatives of Chiang and Yan 118

Around 11:00 AM yesterday morning, Zhang Qun, representative of Military Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Zhao Pilian, representative of Yan Xishan, and Bai Yunti, a member of the Central Committee, visited Wang successively and talked for about 20 minutes. Zhao and Bai left first, and Zhang left after noon. Tang Shengzhi and others went to visit at 2:40 PM in the afternoon and talked for about an hour, leaving at 3:30 PM. At 4:45 PM, French Consul-General Melier also visited Wang to inquire about his departure date.

Zhang Qun's Speech 119

After the heads of various ministries left together at 11:10 AM, Zhang Yuejun, a member of the Central Committee, continued to talk due to other important matters, so he did not leave until after 12:00 PM. Reporters immediately rushed to ask about the meeting with Wang. According to Zhang, Military Committee Chairman Chiang Kai-shek was unable to leave his military duties to come to Shanghai to see Wang off, so he telegraphed him to express his regards on his behalf. Recent rumors that Wang's departure was due to political disagreements were completely inaccurate. President Wang and Chairman Chiang have always cooperated as one person and jointly uphold the reason to set policies to serve the country. This time, Wang's trip to Germany is purely to take advantage of the three-month leave granted by the Central Government to go to recuperate with peace of mind. As for whether he can return to the country within the leave period, it depends on the situation after he arrives in Germany for medical treatment. It cannot be predicted at the moment. If the doctor can determine the source of the disease, prepare the medicine, and return to the country to take it, then Wang can return to the country before the leave expires.

Luo Wengan talks to reporters after visiting Wang (Photo by Li Zunyong)

Luo Wengan's Speech 120

Minister of Foreign Affairs Luo Wengan arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and made the following statement to the reporters who visited him: "I (Luo self-identified) came to Shanghai this time because President Wang is leaving the country to recuperate and is about to depart. I came with my government colleagues to see him off and discuss the diplomatic situation. The Lytton Report is of course also one of the issues discussed." When a reporter asked what the government's attitude was towards the Lytton Report and whether it had decided on a policy, Luo said that President Wang had already pointed out the main points of the government's attitude towards the Lytton Report in his farewell speech. What I want to say now is that although the government's method of dealing with this case has been agreed upon, the application of it still needs to be adapted to circumstances, according to the situation. But my country has a firm principle that will never change, which is the four principles that I declared to China and foreign countries on August 28 this year. This statement has attracted the close attention of all countries in the world. The most important of these is [The reasonable way to resolve the current situation must be based on the letter and spirit of the Covenant of the League of Nations, the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and the Nine-Power Treaty, and the sovereignty of China, while at the same time ensuring the permanent peace of the Far East is a necessary condition]. In short, the steps may vary according to the time, but the principles will remain consistent. What I can tell you today is the consistent principles that the government adheres to. As for the detailed steps, I am sorry that I cannot announce them at this time.

Wang's mother-in-law, Mrs. Chen, visits Wang at Chu's residence (Photo by Li Zunyong)

A Certain Central Committee Member Expresses 121

Wang's trip to Germany this time was granted three months' leave by the Central Government. During this period, Vice President Song will continue to act as President of the Executive Yuan. The previous report that the issue of the President of the Executive Yuan would be discussed at the Third Plenary Session, and that Mr. Sun Zhesheng would succeed as President, was questioned by a reporter from the Central News Agency, who met with a member of the Central Committee yesterday. According to the conversation, the date of the Third Plenary Session has been decided by the previous Central Standing Committee and will be convened on December 1st or 15th. There is no need to raise the issue of the President of the Executive Yuan for discussion. Wang's leave is entirely for medical treatment, and it is different from the rumors of negativity or disagreement. Therefore, the above-mentioned rumors are merely speculations and should not be believed. Regarding Mr. Wu Tiyun's trip north, there are also various speculations from the outside world. However, as far as I know, Mr. Wu expressed that the Central Government's attitude towards the League of Nations and the report of the investigation team was very proper, and his own opinions were consistent with the Central Government.

Wang Jingwei's Speech 122

Wang issued the following statement last night: "(Question) I just saw your speech advocating unity and deeply criticizing local civil wars caused by conflicts over territory. This is indeed the common feeling of the Chinese people, but now civil wars are breaking out in Shandong and Sichuan. What are your thoughts on this?" "(Answer) The current situation of local warlords' separatism has not been completely broken, and the central government has not been able to reach a strong position. This is the current reality and cannot be denied. However, I think that the central government should be clear about right and wrong, distinguish between right and wrong, and start with persuasion, followed by coercion. If the people of the whole country can rise up to help the central government, then this kind of civil war can be stopped. My consultations with Chairman Chiang and President Song are roughly the same. I heard that the Shandong matter has turned around. The situation in Sichuan is complicated, even more than in Shandong. Sichuan's fertile land, large population, and abundant products are only used to support the warlords' separatism, which is really hateful. In February and March this year, the central government had a plan to order the generals in Sichuan to send troops to participate in the anti-Japanese and communist suppression, but unfortunately it was constrained by the status quo and could not be realized. In recent months, the border affairs of Xikang have not been settled, and although the military has repeatedly reported victories, it has not yet been completely successful. Suddenly, this civil war has broken out, and its impact on the border affairs is not small. As for the laughter and abuse from strong neighbors, the loss of international sympathy, and the current diplomatic relations, there is no need to say more. I think that the central government should strictly order the generals to defend their original defenses and wait for investigation, and at the same time send high-ranking officials to thoroughly investigate and determine the method, so that they can all abide by it. Those who do not obey orders should have their crimes announced and abandoned by the world." 6:00 PM on October 21

Regulations on Consular Certification of Cargo Manifests 129

Jianghai Customs Announces Again Yesterday

The regulations on the issuance of consular certified cargo manifests by Chinese consulates abroad, previously approved by the Ministry of Finance, were implemented on August 18th by a public notice issued by the Jianghai Customs. Now, the Jianghai Customs, considering that there are still matters that should be noted in the regulations, issued Public Notice No. 1247 by the Commissioner of Customs, Luo Fude, yesterday, for the information of merchants, stating: "Regarding the matter of public notice, the regulations on the issuance of consular certified cargo manifests by consulates of the Republic of China abroad were announced on August 18th of this year. The following are the matters that should be noted regarding these regulations, for the information of all merchants. Special notice is hereby given. (1) The regulations stipulate that the minimum value of goods exempt from consular certification of cargo manifests is 200 yuan in national currency, which has now been stipulated to be equivalent to 110 customs gold units. Furthermore, the minimum value of goods exempt from consular certification of cargo manifests should be based on the Free on Board (F.O.B.) price, with the exception of goods imported from Japan, Korea, Taiwan, and other Japanese locations. The minimum loan value exempt from consular certification of cargo manifests remains 200 yuan in national currency, not 110 customs gold units. (2) Personal belongings carried by passengers, if not for the purpose of resale, do not require a consular certified cargo manifest, even if the value reaches or exceeds 200 yuan in national currency. (3) If, at the time of shipment, it is confirmed that the entire shipment is destined for a specific importer in a specific port in China, only one consular certified cargo manifest is required, regardless of how the goods are transshipped in batches upon arrival at Chinese ports. (4) For foreign goods transported into various trading ports in China via the Dalian Leased Territory, they should be required to present their certified cargo manifests. If products from the Dalian Leased Territory are transported into various trading ports, merchants may pay five customs gold units to the import customs to obtain a supplementary consular certified cargo manifest, and avoid penalties.

Telegrams from Various Parties Regarding the Sichuan War 132

Liu Wenhui's Telegram; Liu Wenhui's Telegram of the 16th to Chairman Lin of the National Government, Chairman Chiang, and various parties states: "Privately, internal strife does not cease, and foreign insults arrive repeatedly. The entire nation, from top to bottom, is heartbroken. Although Sichuan Province has been plagued by frequent years of unrest, it has fortunately achieved temporary peace. As one humbly entrusted with border defense, I am increasingly cautious. I have spared no effort to eliminate the seeds of chaos and seek governance. The military commanders of all armies, sharing these difficult and precarious concerns, also have the friendship of harmonious cooperation. And Liu Xiang, the commander of the 21st Army, who is stationed in Chongqing and bears greater responsibility, if he can cooperate fairly and sincerely, it will not be difficult to proceed step by step, to communicate upwards to the central government and to comfort the people downwards. Therefore, within the past few years, I have repeatedly traveled to Luzhou and Chongqing, going back and forth to negotiate, hoping for his acceptance. I have not hesitated to lay bare my sincerity and express my humility. The details of this process have already been reported to your government and are already known to you. Unexpectedly, there are ulterior motives that are difficult to fathom. Since the reorganization of the provincial government, the state of division has remained unchanged. The awakening period... In the army-garrisoned areas, once sincere advocacy is initiated, they will all cooperate to revitalize the situation. However, in the corner of eastern Sichuan, the original system is followed, and now it is even more intensified. I have always been an advocate for peace and have always been accommodating, fearing even the slightest dispute that would be scorned by those with understanding. Moreover, with the national crisis at hand and the Kangding affairs pressing, it is essential for the entire nation to unite in ceasing disputes and resisting foreign aggression. How can we allow the Sichuan that has been peaceful for several years to not focus on resisting foreign aggression but instead allow internal strife to develop, leading to reproach from the central government and loss of sympathy from the people? Yet, I do not know what Liu Xiang, the military commander, intends. With a heart to stir up chaos, he secretly ordered Luo Zezhou and Li Jiayu, two divisions, to suddenly launch a large-scale military action on the 1st of this month, crossing the border to attack Shunqing and Lidu, where my troops are stationed. I have truthfully and repeatedly reported the actual situation to your government on the Jiayuan and Shan days. Fortunately, I have received your clear understanding and successive telegrams ordering Military Commander Liu Xiang to take responsibility for stopping the action and ordering the troops under Li and Luo to retreat to their original defense and await the central government's decision. Furthermore, I have received numerous telegrams from all sectors of the party, government, military, and people within and outside the province, lamenting the wrongs of war and hoping for compliance with the order to cease hostilities. Those with even a little conscience should feel remorse. Upon investigation, it is also known that the central government is clear-sighted and that the instigator is difficult to hold accountable. Initially, they instigated Li and Luo to provoke me, hoping that if I retaliated, they could refer to it as a conflict between me and Li and Luo, and then ask the central government to take responsibility for stopping it, thereby taking advantage of armed mediation to gain profit. The reports, the telegrams between Liu Xiang and Li and Luo, can be reviewed and confirmed. Therefore, I respectfully obeyed the clear orders and retreated step by step, always strictly ordering my troops to defend their original positions. However, Li Jiayu's troops fiercely attacked Shuncheng on the Yu day, and some 21st Army troops, under the guise of Li and Luo's banners, mingled among them, assisting in the attack. On one hand, they picked on my shortcomings to confuse the public. On the other hand, they ordered their troops to launch simultaneous attacks on Yongchuan, Dazu, and Jiangjin, where my troops are stationed, expanding the war zone. This is truly something I cannot understand, and it is something the entire nation sighs in unison. I have diligently performed my duties day and night, and I believe that I have not offended Chongqing. Even if there are differences in political views due to different positions, I have always been tolerant and receptive to criticism. If I am found to be wrong, I will accept correction. Otherwise, I can report the facts to the central government, and it is not impossible to make them public. Why must I launch an unwarranted war, causing the central government to worry and the entire nation to criticize, laughing at foreigners and bringing disaster to the people during a time when the entire nation is against war? Furthermore, I have read the telegrams from Tang Shizun and other division commanders of the 21st Army, fabricating many names, creating regulations, and seeking the consent of various armies. Their intention to establish independent rule and disregard the central government, sparing no effort to resort to force and war, is now abundantly clear. The truth and falsehood can be seen in the telegrams from Chen Dingxun and other division commanders, which are clearly clarified. I will not reiterate the lengthy arguments. However, their fabrication of the situation to coerce the central government and their intention to deceive the central government in order to manipulate public opinion are particularly deceitful, and everyone can see it. At a time when the entire nation is calling for peace, I am working hard on the Kangding defense, but they are allowed to act willfully, destroying the overall situation and harming themselves. I say this with extreme pain and no tears to shed. Your judgment is clear, and your authority is decisive. Please investigate the cause of this incident and the locations of the two battles, and you will know that my words are not false. The responsibility lies where it belongs. Quickly issue strict orders to Military Commander Liu Xiang, ordering him to comply with repeated orders, stop Li and Luo, and hold them accountable for their due punishment. Also, strictly restrain his troops from using this as an excuse to launch a war and expand the battlefield. I am incompetent, causing a potential conflict among close relatives. I am ashamed of my lack of virtue and dare not tell others. However, I am also a military commander of the national army and a territorial official of a province. If those who disobey the orders of the central government are allowed to arbitrarily use force without being held accountable, and if a prompt decision is not made, discipline will be swept away, and the flames of war will increase, and there will be no end to it. Considering the innocent people calling and crying for an end to the war, I have no way to avoid it and cannot stand idly by. I only ask that you dispatch a senior official to Sichuan as soon as possible to implement the cessation of hostilities. If you are concerned that my allegations are not true, once investigated, the truth will be revealed, and the matter will be handled appropriately. Urgent words are presented with fear and trembling, not daring to express the extent of my shame and awaiting your orders. Liu Wenhui bows."

Citizens' Volunteer Army Forms Peddling Group After Demobilization to Sell Goods and Donate to the Volunteer Army 139

Minde Factory Sacrifices Profits

Balancing Public and Private Interests

The Citizens' Volunteer Army for the Defense of Shanghai against the Japanese has demobilized and returned, and many of its members have lost their jobs. They have now organized a volunteer peddling group to sell goods, with 30% of the profits going to support the Northeast Volunteer Army. The local Volunteer Army Support Association is publishing this notice to introduce them. The following is the original text: [Notice from the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association Regarding the Volunteer Peddling Group Selling Minde Factory's Tiger Brand Yarn Rope and Donating the Profits to the Volunteer Army] Some Shanghai merchants participated in the Citizens' Volunteer Army for the Defense of Shanghai against the Japanese and fought the enemy for the country. Since the ceasefire and their return, their original positions have been taken by others, and they all need to find new livelihoods. They have organized a peddling group, now officially named the Volunteer Peddling Corps. The Minde Yarn Rope Factory has agreed to provide its Tiger Brand yarn rope, which is used by various factories and shops for bundling goods, to the group for peddling. After deducting the cost, the profits will be divided into ten parts, with three parts donated to the Northeast Volunteer Army and the remaining seven parts used for the living expenses of the peddling group. Minde Factory's yarn rope comes in two thicknesses, each bundle containing 6,000 or 12,000 feet of yarn rope, with a selling price of 5 yuan each. The quality is strong, and the colors are complete, making it very practical. Our association recognizes the difficult situation of the Volunteer Peddling Corps, who are still willing to support the Volunteer Army, and also appreciates the generosity and righteousness of the Minde Factory, which is sacrificing profits. Therefore, we are happy to introduce them and will stamp the order books. The group will also notify our association with one copy from the four-part order form to facilitate auditing and ensure prudence. We hope that major factories and shops will actively purchase their products, not only to promote national goods and maintain people's livelihoods but also to support the Volunteer Army in recovering lost territory, achieving multiple benefits in one stroke. Your consideration is greatly appreciated.

Fresh Pork Industry Representatives Petition in Beijing 144

Actively Opposing the Pork Tax in Jiangbei

The fresh pork industry associations of various counties in Jiangsu Province have reported that the business tax bureaus of Jingru and Tai counties in Jiangbei have suddenly established branch offices in various ports of those counties since September 21st of this year, totaling 16 offices, specifically to levy business taxes on pigs passing through. Initially, they sent police to extort money, and then they detained goods to force payment. Special letters were sent to industry associations in various counties to nominate representatives to come to Shanghai to form a joint office and actively resist. Recently, they decided to nominate more than 40 representatives to form a petition group to petition in Beijing and the provinces. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, they held a farewell meeting at the association's headquarters. Representatives from various counties gave speeches of encouragement. Petition representative Xin Wenyao stood up to reply, stating that his colleagues would do their best to resist and strive to achieve the goal of abolishing the tax, and would not fail the expectations of everyone.

Movement for Wage Increase by Round Wood Workers 145

Various round wood shops in this city, specializing in making wooden buckets and basins, employ workers whose wages are 3 jiao and 5 fen per day. The workers, believing that the cost of living has been increasing recently and that their wages are not enough to cover their expenses, have been requesting wage increases from their respective shop owners, without success. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, they convened workers from various shops in the north and south of the city at the First Spring restaurant outside the Old North Gate to discuss the matter, and invited shop owners to the meeting. A representative of the workers said that the wages of workers in the woodenware industry are 6 or 7 jiao per day, or at least 5 jiao, but the wages of the round wood workers are very low, only 3 jiao and 5 fen per day. If they stop working for one day, there is no income. With prices rising for everything, it is really difficult to support a family with their current wages. Today, we have specially invited the shop owners to come here to request a wage increase of 1 jiao per day. Please consider the workers' plight and grant our request. The shop owners, on the other hand, said that business is currently sluggish, business is small, the cost of goods is high, and it is difficult to increase prices, so they are barely surviving. The workers also know this, and the requested wage increase is too large, and it concerns all of the businesses and cannot be agreed to. The workers said that the requested wage increase of 1 jiao has been discussed publicly and is the smallest amount. The two sides discussed the matter for a long time, but there was no result. It is now decided to hold another meeting another day.

The Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters Sent Personnel to Investigate the Labor Strike of Taikoo Middle Cabin Crew 146

Will Convene Both Parties for Mediation

The stewards on the Yangtze River boats of the British-owned Taikoo Company have joined the Middle Cabin Branch of the Seamen's Union. Previously, the company's comprador suddenly requested the company's managers to limit the number of stewards on each boat to a maximum of 50 people and issued five service rules, causing the entire crew to express their dissatisfaction. They reported this to the Seamen's Union and petitioned the Central Government to strictly prohibit it. The day before yesterday, direct negotiations between labor and management broke down. The labor side then joined forces with stewards from other friendly boats and planned to petition the municipal government today (the 22nd). Yesterday, the Municipal Party Headquarters heard about this and, fearing that the labor strike would escalate, sent Dai Yongchan, a cadre from the People's Education Section, to investigate everything. Wei Kuisheng, a standing committee member of the union, met with him, reported the details, and requested assistance. Cadre Dai immediately expressed his acceptance and promised to convene both parties for mediation at a later date. Mr. Wei expressed his satisfaction and promised to automatically cancel today's petition.

Cable of Japanese Ship Broke, Killing Postal Worker 150

The Japanese mail ship Hakusan Maru was docked at the Osaka Wharf. The local postal bureau sent three postal workers to the wharf to pick up mail. One person was knocked into the Huangpu River by a Japanese ship and drowned. This matter is being negotiated. The circumstances are recorded as follows:

Picking Up Mail 151

The Japanese Post Office's European route mail ship Hakusan Maru arrived in Shanghai on the 19th. Because the Wayside Wharf was full, it changed its berth to the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. The Shengjing Maru ship of the Osaka Company also arrived in Shanghai from Dalian and Qingdao on the same day and docked at the same place. More than 30 bags of mail were transported on the ship. The post office sent three postal workers to the ship to pick them up and transport them to the main bureau for distribution.

Japanese Ship Causes Trouble 152

When the three postal workers arrived at the Shengjing Maru ship, the Hakusan Maru was docked on the same wharf. It was the morning of the 19th. The mail inside the Shengjing Maru ship was being unloaded from the ship. The three postal workers were also checking the mail when, unexpectedly, a cable rope of the Hakusan Maru suddenly came loose and leaped up from below with great force. All three postal workers were violently knocked into the Huangpu River by the cable.

One Person Drowned 153

When the three postal workers were knocked into the Huangpu River by the Hakusan Maru's loose cable, small boats and civilian boats near the wharf competed to rescue them. However, all three people sank to the bottom of the river at first. Fortunately, after hundreds of attempts, two people were rescued. One person was missing and could not be rescued in time. He drowned immediately. The post office has now sternly negotiated with the Japanese Post Office.

Mother Serves Jail Time for Daughter 155

Negligence of Female Warden

Mother and Daughter Conspire to Substitute

Song Bingzheng, a detective from the Narcotics Division of the Public Concession Police Department, cracked down on a smoking den at 273 Jiujiang Road on September 6th. Among the arrested opium smokers were two women from Jiangsu Province: Ji Qian, 39 years old, and Wang Bao, a young woman of marriageable age. They claimed to be mother and daughter. The police transferred the two women to the female detention center of the First Special District Court for detention. The next morning, Judge Feng interrogated them clearly. He sentenced Wang Bao to one month of imprisonment and a fine of 20 yuan. If she could not pay, she could serve the sentence in prison. Li Qian was not addicted to opium and should be released. After the judgment, the police were ordered to take them back to the detention center for the warden to execute the sentence. At that time, the acting warden was Ms. Ye Huihua. It is said that Ye was transferred from the Hangzhou prison. There is another warden position. On that day, it happened to be the day for inmates to meet with their families. Many family members of the inmates entered and exited the detention center. Li Qian and her daughter took advantage of this opportunity to discuss a plan to substitute one for another. When Ye called the roll, Li Qian impersonated Wang Bao, and Wang Bao impersonated Li Qian. As a result, the person who should have been in prison was at large, and the person who should have been released was imprisoned. As for the reason why they used this cunning trick, Li Qian considered herself old and had no ability to work. She was not addicted to opium, so being in prison would have no impact. However, if her daughter was in prison, not only would she suffer financial losses, but she would also suffer mentally. Therefore, she hoped to take a risk and get lucky. Unexpectedly, Ye was negligent and was deceived. Until recently, after the newly appointed female warden Shen Ying took office, she checked the female inmates in prison. When calling Wang Bao's name, she saw that the age on the register was 34 years old, but observing her appearance, although she was not old and frail, she did not look young either. Therefore, she became suspicious and interrogated her strictly. Li Qian knew that it was difficult to hide the truth, so she told the truth. Director Shen immediately reported to the warden of the Second Branch Prison, who forwarded it to Shen, the President of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, who instructed the First Special Court to investigate the matter strictly. The prosecutor's office of the court commissioned Prosecutor Zhan Liangce to conclude the investigation. Ye Huihua could not escape the blame for negligence. Li Qian helped her escape, and she deserved the punishment even more. He filed a lawsuit for questioning, while Wang Bao has been engaging in prostitution since she was released. She would wait for customers every night on the streets and was arrested. After being sentenced by the court, she was handed over to the prosecutor's office. Prosecutor Zhan also investigated her and filed a public prosecution together with Ye and others, accusing Ye of violating Article 172, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, and Li Qian and Wang Bao of violating Article 170, Paragraph 1 and Article 171, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday, Judge Wu Zhen opened the court and interrogated the three defendants. Qian Xunjiu, a lawyer from the Public Works Bureau, also attended the hearing. Ye Yaohua hired a lawyer to defend himself, admitting that there were many people entering and exiting on the day of the inmates' family visit, and he was negligent in checking, which led to this mistake. The defendant has been serving in the Hangzhou prison for many years and has never made a mistake. He requested leniency. The other two defendants admitted that they had colluded with each other to deceive and escape. Judge Wu then ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and await sentencing.

War Zone Temporary Relief Loan Office

The Wusong Temporary Relief Loan Office of the Shanghai War Zone Rehabilitation Committee, attached to the Municipal Committee Office, was officially opened yesterday to handle the registration of the poor.
