Gang Fight Among Workers at Dada Wharf 158

Due to Refusal to Allow Scabs to Work

More Than a Dozen People Injured in the Fight

The dock workers in the Dada Wharf area of Nanshi have been managed by Foreman Zhang Jinkui. Whenever the Dada Steamboat Company's ships arrive at the port, Zhang dispatches a group of foremen to lead the workers to transport goods on the ships. However, whenever the work is busy, all the workers are not enough to handle it, so he recruits a group of scab workers from Pudong to help out in Puxi. Yesterday at noon, a tragic fight occurred due to Zhang Jinkui's refusal to allow the scab workers to work, and more than a dozen people were seriously injured. The details are as follows: At about 12 noon yesterday, when the Dada Steamboat Company's Dahe ship arrived at the port, Zhang Jinkui ordered Xie Zhaoming, a foreman from Yangzhou, to lead more than 30 workers to transport goods on the Dahe ship. Suddenly, more than 30 scab workers from Pudong also wanted to join the work. The Puxi workers, because the work at Dada Wharf has always been contracted by them, would not allow others to come and interfere. Therefore, they immediately stopped the work, while the Pudong scab workers, because when Puxi is busy, there are not enough workers, they recruit them to help out. When the work is light, they are arbitrarily dismissed. Therefore, they are determined to have a meal for everyone and still want to transport goods. As a result, the Pudong workers and the Puxi workers first competed for the goods and had a quarrel. Then, they disagreed and started a big fight. They saw the workers on both sides holding weapons such as sticks and iron hooks on the dock, glaring and full of murderous intent, ignoring life and death, and beating each other randomly. As a result, many people were injured on both sides. When the water patrol team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau saw this, they immediately stepped forward and took nine Puxi workers, including Shen Youshan, Cui Tongjiang, Fan Qikang, Zhang Shengtai, Xu Yuguan, Wang Jiuyou, Zhang Dianchen, Zhang Wenxiong, and Xu Erzhong, all from Yangzhou, back to the team for interrogation. They sent 11 injured workers from both sides to the Nanshi Hospital of the Red Cross. There were a total of seven injured people from Pudong, including Xu Baoqing, a 27-year-old from Yangzhou, who was injured in the head, Wang Asong, a 28-year-old from Yangzhou, who was injured in the head, Yang Buchen, a 26-year-old from Huaicheng, who was injured in the head and arms, Wang Heshun, a 21-year-old from Huaicheng, who was injured in the back, Ding Wanlin, a 28-year-old from Huaicheng, who was injured in the head, Yang San, a 45-year-old from Huaicheng, who was injured in the head, and Bao Changxian, a 24-year-old from Yangzhou, who was injured in the head. Among them, Yang Buchen was the most seriously injured and may be in danger of death. There were a total of four people from Puxi who were injured, including Qiu Hengyu, 27 years old, injured in the head, Yan Fengzhen, 29 years old, injured in the head and back, Zhu Xiaozu, 24 years old, injured in the back, and Jiao Guanglong, 27 years old, injured in the back. All of the above are from Yangzhou. Captain Zhu interrogated them and submitted the case to the Judicial Section for review that night.

Public Concession 159

Police Report for September

Amnesty of Prisoners The Public Works Bureau's police report for September states that in June of this year, the Chinese government promulgated an amnesty decree. According to this decree, the First Special District Court approved the release of 1,427 prisoners from the prisons in the concession from July 16th. Among them, 448 were repeat offenders, 365 had old cases but were not considered repeat offenders, and 614 were first-time offenders. Twelve of those released were foreigners. The crimes committed by the released prisoners ranged from murder, kidnapping, robbery, abduction, and sedition to communist crimes and theft. Some had been convicted up to 19 times. In addition, 80 people who had been released and re-offended were arrested.

Crime Statistics In September, 1,542 reported crimes, an increase of 127 from August (but a decrease of 65 from the same month last year). The increase was due to the release of a large number of prisoners and the cooler weather. However, the number of arrests also increased, totaling 1,752, an increase of 158 from August. In addition, 99 people were arrested for old cases, and 73 were arrested on behalf of officials outside the concession. In September, there were 5 murders, 1 homicide, 1 armed kidnapping, 3 bombing incidents, and 40 armed robberies. This number is 17 more than in August. However, the value of the items stolen was mostly small. In addition, there were 7 robbery cases and 59 theft cases. The police department paid special attention to this because many habitual thieves were released due to the amnesty. There were 28 burglary cases this month. Larceny cases decreased significantly this month, while bicycle theft cases increased. There were 94 snatching cases, nearly double the number of last month, but 78 people were arrested. The reported value of stolen property this month was over 177,000 yuan, and the value of recovered property was over 58,000 yuan.

Communist Party Cases This month, 2,761 pieces of communist propaganda were seized, including 37 types of leaflets, which were newly discovered. The texts mostly concerned the anniversary of the International Youth Movement, the Manchurian problem, and the eradication of communists. Some also denounced White Russians for obstructing strikes. The Communist Party organs searched three places and arrested 12 Chinese, who have not yet been tried.

Strikes There were 5 strikes in the concession this month, involving 1,427 workers and resulting in 484 lost workdays. The factories involved were the Public Bus Company, Neiwaimian Factories 3, 6, and 7, and one tannery and one silk factory.

Film Censorship Police officers inspected 43 feature films and 38 short films. Three feature films and one short film were passed after being censored, and there were no problems with the rest.

Traffic Accidents 968 cases of traffic violations were prosecuted (51 foreigners and 917 Chinese). In addition, more than 3,300 minor cases were given warnings. There were 1,116 traffic accidents this month, with 399 people injured and 10 deaths. Traffic accidents involved bicycles 202 times, and in 73 of these cases, it was proven that the cyclist was at fault.

Emergency Meeting of Various Organizations in Hongkou 160

Report Cites Letter from Mr. Anson Opposing Telephone Price Increase

Organizations such as the Shanghai Citizens' Federation, the Hongkou District Branches, and the business associations of Hanbi Road, Dongyouheng Road, Yuanfang Road, Suzhou Road, North Shaanxi Road, Yinxianggang, Huade Road, East Broadway Road, Haining Road, North Jiangxi Road, East Xihuade Road, Avenue Edward VII, Jielu, Yuezhou Road, Wuzhou Road, Jiaxing Road, Yangshupu Road, etc., held an emergency joint meeting of representatives at 2 pm yesterday to discuss countermeasures against the telephone company's demand that fees be paid according to the new regulations, with a deadline of the 21st, and its threat to disconnect the lines. More than 20 people, including Zhang Yumen, attended, and Zhang Xianfang was elected chairman. After the report was made, the following matters were discussed: (1) The telephone price increase case. It was resolved that: (A) A declaration should be issued; (B) Another letter should be sent to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to lodge a serious protest and stop the disconnection. The declaration and the letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association are recorded below.

Declaration Opposing Telephone Price Increase Shanghai is China's first commercial port. In recent years, commerce has been exhausted, and coupled with the war, the market has become even more desolate, finance has declined, and the people are struggling to survive. Instead of seeking material reductions to help each other through difficult times, so as to save this declining situation, all public utilities, which are in a position of coexistence and co-prosperity, should exercise the method of mediation. Telephones are one of the public utilities. How can the company unilaterally raise prices and the Public Works Bureau ignore public opinion, follow their lead, and arbitrarily raise prices? They did not publicize it in advance, nor did they seek the consent of the Chinese taxpayers, violating legal principles and human feelings, and opening an unprecedented example of price increases, which is infuriating. The company cited Mr. Anson's proposal in 1929. Now Mr. Anson has sent a letter to the Board of Directors of the Public Works Bureau, saying that "the original intention was to test whether the company could keep its promise" and that "the pre-testing was only a trial." How can the Public Works Bureau seriously regard it as a passed case? Moreover, the market today is not what it used to be, and Mr. Anson also said, "[However, the economic changes during this period mentioned above have not been taken into account]," etc. We should know that Shanghai's current economic situation is declining, so how can we increase the burden on the citizens? This time, the opposition to the telephone price increase is based on public justice. The Zilin News reported the other day that Americans also oppose the price increase. Therefore, the opposition to the telephone price increase has become a consensus among Chinese and Western people. According to the report, there is even a record of the Public Works Bureau guaranteeing a one-point interest rate, which is even more shocking. Now, in the core calculation of the price increase, they say that it only accounts for 8%. We are afraid that after this year, it will have to be increased again next year. If the price is increased again and again, how can the citizens bear it? Looking to the future, for the sake of the future, we must insist on opposing it to the end. Let us encourage each other. This is our declaration.

Letter of Protest Against Disconnection to the Taxpayers' Association (abridged above) We have repeatedly struggled against the telephone price increase. Under this protest, the company even threatened to collect the increased fees and gave a deadline of the 21st of this month to disconnect the lines, etc. This illegal method has made the Chinese taxpayers' association very angry. The company is using the Public Works Bureau's approval as an iron case and is obviously using one-sided words. The Public Works Bureau is exercising dictatorship, which our Chinese taxpayers can hardly tolerate. Now, let us list its illegal points: (1) Arbitrarily raising prices without publicizing the facts in advance; (2) All price increases are timely, so how can the past period be increased at the time of billing and included; (3) Using the Public Works Bureau as a kissing permit, the price increase was not subject to the public opinion of all Chinese taxpayers; (4) Compulsory execution is not allowed by law. We are very legally paying the same fees as before under protest. How can we collect the price increase and disconnect the lines at will? If we owe money, we must also pursue it through legal procedures and implement coercive illegal methods; (5) According to Mr. Anson's proposal in 1929, three years have passed. At this time of commercial decline and economic exhaustion, it is too much to suddenly increase its price without considering the situation. Based on the above facts and the opposition to the price increase, the just demands that our Chinese taxpayers should have are that, before the protest period is resolved, paying the same price is the only proper way. We firmly oppose the company's illegal act of limiting the disconnection. We will send another letter to your association to fight to the end based on reason and strive to achieve the final goal, and we must strictly stop the disconnection to comfort public opinion.

Two Injured Western Detectives in Critical Condition

The one who was injured in the right arm had his arm amputated due to the severity of the injury, and it is still difficult to predict whether he will survive. The bullet has not yet been removed from the one who was injured in the leg, which is very dangerous. At that time, the police department seized a Mauser pistol, an automatic pistol, and a small Browning pistol, as well as 240 yuan in banknotes. A diamond ring was also found on the defendant. Jiang Huixing confessed that he knew Ma Zhengxiang and was introduced by Ma to Wang Acai and others to discuss the matter. The firearms were borrowed by Ma from Kong Rongsheng. When the robbery took place, I went to knock on the door and pretended to be a mahjong company. Someone was talking to Mr. Wang (i.e., the victim). When the detectives arrived, I was going to open fire and resist arrest, but the bullet jammed, which led to my arrest. Judge Fu verified the confession and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further interrogation at a later date.

A Mediator Assaulted

Following mediation, Zhu was ordered to move by a set deadline. Unexpectedly, after leaving the station and returning home, Sun resorted to violence, throwing Zhu's belongings outside, demanding her immediate departure. Another quarrel broke out. Lou Liansheng, residing at No. 5 in the same lane, along with other neighbors, watched as Zhu, heavily pregnant, jumped and screamed, fearing for her fetus. The police chief ordered Sun to be treated at Renji Hospital. Meanwhile, Lou was sent to the Second Special Court, charged under Article 293 of the criminal code for assault. Plaintiff Sun Shengchang recounted the assault, gesticulating wildly as if suffering from a nervous disorder. Defendant Lou Liansheng denied the assault.

Qian Zubei's Trial Suspended

Qian Zubei, known as the "Red Pill King," alias Guo Lian, nicknamed "Little Shandong," previously established a large-scale illegal red pill operation at No. 46 Ruifu Lane, Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, selling over ten thousand taels worth of pills monthly. A French detective from the French Concession police discovered the operation and, accompanied by Chinese detective Li Liansheng, arrested Qian along with manager Shi Yinbao, associates Chen Degen, Yu Jinkang, and suspects Yuan Kexia and Cao Nanshan. All were sent to the Second Special Court. After questioning, Qian was ordered to post a bail of eight thousand yuan, Chen Degen three thousand yuan, and the other four one thousand yuan each, pending further investigation. Qian disappeared after posting bail. The court issued a second summons and declared the debate concluded, setting a date for the verdict. Details of Qian Zubei's bail forfeiture and arrest warrant were previously reported. Yesterday, Judge Xiong presided over the verdict at the First Criminal Court, sentencing Shi Yinbao to one year of imprisonment and a fine of five hundred yuan for selling opium substitutes; Chen Degen, alias Chen Degen, to six months of imprisonment and a fine of fifty yuan for aiding in the sale of opium substitutes; Yu Jinkang to eight months of imprisonment and a fine of one hundred yuan for providing premises for opium substitute smoking with intent to profit. The confiscated red pills were to be forfeited. Yuan Kexia and Cao Nanshan were acquitted. Qian Zubei's trial was suspended.

Fire on Tingsi Road in the Southern City 171

Raging Flames Extinguished in an Instant

The Power of the "Invincible Brand" Chemical Fire Extinguisher

A fire broke out at Gu Longxing's store on Tingsi Road, west of the Southern City Local Court, at 7:00 AM on the 20th, originating from a cotton pile in the back building. The fire spread to the roof, with flames leaping and sparks flying. Fortunately, the adjacent Family Industrial Society quickly used an "Invincible Brand" chemical fire extinguisher to combat the flames. The device proved extremely convenient: when inverted, the chemical foam sprayed out through the hose, extinguishing the fire instantly. The store was located in a remote area, and the fire brigade had not yet noticed the blaze. Without the rapid action of the "Invincible Brand" chemical fire extinguisher, not only would the store have been lost, but several neighboring businesses would have been consumed as well.

Fire in a Straw Shed in Xujiazhai, Zhabei Last Night 172

Spreading to Over Sixty Buildings

Around 10:10 last night, a fire broke out in a straw hut belonging to a Zhao family in the Jiangbei slum area of Xujiazhai, behind the New Infant Hall on Zhongxing Road, Zhabei. The fire quickly spread to neighboring huts, causing an uncontrollable blaze that lit up the sky. Fire trucks from various sections of Zhabei rushed to the scene, but as one fire was extinguished, another would ignite, threatening to engulf the entire slum. Fortunately, firefighters bravely persevered and gradually extinguished the blaze, fully extinguishing it by 12:30 AM. A total of over sixty straw huts were destroyed. The responsible party is currently at large, and police from the Fourth District Office are searching for and arresting the suspect for investigation. Many affected slum dwellers are now sleeping in the open, in a dire situation.

Central Bank Inspection Report 173

140th Inspection

The Central Bank's 140th Inspection Report on Issuance Reserves states: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserves for convertible notes issued by the Bank. On October 20, 1932, Supervisor Yu Qiaqing conducted the 140th inspection at the Bank's Issuance Bureau. The results are announced as follows: (A) Total value of silver dollar convertible notes issued: 30,066,354 silver dollars, including 27,412,874 silver dollar notes and 3,250,980 subsidiary coins. Total value of convertible note reserves: 30,066,354 silver dollars, including 24,849,854 silver dollars in cash. This cash reserve is held in the Bank's issuing vault: 22,217,402.74 silver dollars, in branch banks in various ports: 1,460,528 silver dollars, and with fellow banks: 1,171,923.26 silver dollars. Guarantee reserve: 5,814,000 silver dollars. (B) Total value of customs gold unit convertible notes issued: 425,000 customs gold units. Total value of customs gold unit convertible note reserves: 425,000 customs gold units, including 170,000 US dollars deposited with fellow banks in this port, valued at 0.40 customs gold units, totaling 425,000 customs gold units. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's regulations on convertible notes, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. The Central Bank Supervisory Council, October 20, 1932.

Municipal Self-Government Preparatory Committee Invites Bids for Printed Materials 174

Since being ordered to prepare for self-government below the district level, the Municipal Self-Government Preparatory Committee has been actively working, sparing no effort. All investigation election implementation regulations have been drafted and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval by the Ministry of Interior, as previously reported. The committee is now inviting bids for printing investigation-related materials in preparation for starting the investigation. The bidding registration period is from today until 12:00 PM on October 31st. The public bid opening will be held at the committee at 10:00 AM on November 1st. The total standard price has been set at 20,500 yuan. Registration begins today until publication in various newspapers. The previous report stating that bidding would begin on October 26th was incorrect. The committee's bidding guidelines are excerpted below: (1) Bidders must first pay a sample fee of 10 yuan at the committee to obtain sample materials, draft samples, and contract drafts for detailed review in preparation for bidding. (2) All sample materials, draft samples, and contract drafts obtained by bidders must be returned, regardless of whether they vote or not. The committee will rely on this to recover the sample fee paid. (3) After a bidder has paid the sample fee to the committee, those who wish to bid must be verified by the committee to ensure that they have the ability to undertake the work before obtaining a bid envelope and bid form. At the same time, a bid deposit of 1,000 yuan must be paid, and the meeting will issue a receipt. (4) Bidders should list the voting prices item by item on the bid form in accordance with the sample regulations, and separate the total number of singles for verification. (For example, the voting price for each item is so much, totaling so much.) (5) Bids that do not use the bid form and envelope of the council or that are not filled in according to the format will be rejected. (6) The bid form and envelope must be filled in clearly item by item, and no alterations may be made. The bidder must affix a seal and signature, and seal it tightly. On the day of the bid, they must personally go to the council and put it into the ballot box. (7) When bidding, the committee will first decide on a standard price, which will be published in the newspapers. At the time of bid opening, the bids will be reviewed separately, and the lowest price that does not exceed the standard price will be the winning bid. (8) The winning bidder shall, within seven days of the announcement, produce a sample according to the specified materials and draft sample, and send it to the meeting for approval, and at the same time pay 10% of the bid price as a contract deposit. If they fail to come to the meeting to sign the contract within the time limit, the bid deposit will be forfeited and the next person will be filled in. (9) Those who are not successful in the bid may withdraw the receipt of their bid deposit after the committee has signed a contract with the winning bidder. (10) Goods shall be delivered on the date specified, and if delayed by one day, 1% of the contract bid price shall be fined per day. If the delay extends to seven days, the contract deposit will be forfeited and bidding will be conducted separately.

To the Editor, In the local news column of your newspaper on the 21st of this month, I read the news item "Forced Divorce, Wife Desperate and Commits Suicide." After reading it, it is slightly inconsistent with the facts. It was the deceased's mother, Mrs. Ye Fan, who came forward to negotiate with Yu Zengrong and filed a criminal lawsuit with the court. Because the deceased's mother was sick in bed, she entrusted me to take care of her, so I made a commitment to the prosecutor to coffin and bury her. The report said (had negotiated with Sister Qian) etc., which must be false rumors. I am sending a special letter to inform you and hope that it will be corrected immediately. To the Chief Editor of Shen Bao, Shi Jiwan, October 21, 1932.

Free Talk

Two or Three Words

Taking a Circuitous Route 191

— Zhan Lu

Taking the direct path was the norm during the Three Dynasties, a golden age long past. In the modern era, however, taking a circuitous route is advocated everywhere. In social engagements, commercial advertising, the major policies of important figures, and various other approaches, no one is willing to do as the people of Suzhou say: dragging logs through a narrow alleyway, straight out. Instead, they must imitate the curvilinear beauty of women, believing that the more circuitous, the more rounded, the more beautiful. In this way, what is said will not fall on deaf ears, like a neverending circle. Alas! Words that do not fall on deaf ears are equivalent to useless words!

Everything can be circuitous: suppose you ask someone for guidance on success or failure, or to judge merits and demerits, it seems that there should be a definite indication; but, according to two anecdotes I have heard, those who give guidance and those who judge can also use a circuitous method to deal with it.

In the old days of the imperial examinations, there were three candidates who asked a certain high monk to predict their success or failure: the high monk did not add any opinion, but only raised one finger. After the candidates left, someone asked the high monk: Can this one finger indicate their success or failure? The monk said: This is a circuitous indication, no matter what, they cannot escape the old monk's one-finger Zen: if all three pass the exam, it means that everything is successful; if all three fail, it means that everything is unsuccessful; if two of the three pass and one fails, it means that one is unsuccessful, and if one of the three passes and two fail, it means that one is successful: no one can escape this all-around one-finger Zen opportunity.

There was also a young woman who sat at a square table with three suitors at the same time; the three men asked the young woman at the same time: Who of us three is better? The young woman came up with a circuitous answer: facing the suitors sitting opposite her, she said: You are good. The tip of her high-heeled leather shoes quietly kicked the feet of the suitors on the left and right under the table, so that all three suitors sitting together felt that the young woman praised them.

Alas! There are no people who take the direct path now; the impartial people and judges of the modern era are expressing the one-finger Zen opportunity there; they are promising the other party with their mouths, and secretly kicking the feet of both parties with their toes.

A Brave General of the 19th Route Army 192

— Hong Yangshan

| General Weng Zhaoyuan |

General Weng Zhaoyuan, loyal and brave in resisting Japan, fighting for national dignity and for the glory of the nation, has long been admired by people at home. He is a graduate of the Japanese Military Academy. After graduation, he went to France to study aviation. Once, during a test flight in Paris, the plane was inverted and about to crash. The audience on the ground thought that there was no hope of survival. If others were in this dangerous situation, they would definitely fall from a high altitude and die, but the general always tried his best to support it, and was finally able to drive the plane to the ground, only injuring his foot.

He used to be a division commander, and then he went to be a soldier for a year. This spirit is really admirable. Now he doesn't have a wife and lives in a house with a monthly rent of more than ten yuan.

When the Shanghai Incident broke out, the general was in charge of the front line, fighting against the Japanese soldiers in Zhabei. The enemy could not enter a step. Later, because Wusong was in urgent need, the general was transferred to defend the area. At that time, the enemy used all its naval, land and air forces to attack Wusong. The general commanded freely and held the fort, using machine guns as artillery to kill the enemy. He said to his subordinates: [We kill the enemy with guns, no guns with bayonets, no bayonets with gun butts, no gun butts with hands and feet.] What tragic words these are. After the 19th Route Army had withdrawn, the general still held the fort and refused to leave. The elders of Wusong told him in tears, persuading him to save his body to serve the country in the future. At this point, he cried bitterly and withdrew his troops, and was still in a battle with the Japanese soldiers for three rounds at China Public School.

This time, General Weng resigned from his position as brigade commander and went abroad to promote aviation and save the country. When he arrived in Shanghai, it was the first day of the school's voluntary military training this semester. He was invited to the school to give a speech, which was full of heroism and filled his eyebrows. In his speech, he said: [Don't be pessimistic about the future of China. We must know that national disasters are not very terrible. The most terrible thing is that everyone does not know how to save it when there is a national disaster! ]

Are You Pursuing Too, Friend? 193

— Ji Xiang

丨For Modern Men丨

Friend, are you married? Do you also feel sexual frustration? Are you pursuing someone? Are you pursuing blindly! Or do you already have a worthy counterpart, and does she also love you? Is your face handsome? Is your suit elegant? Do you have money in your pocket? Does she find these things satisfying? Otherwise, if you don't have even these basic requirements for romance, then I advise you to be quiet! Your pursuit will only lead to disappointment, and you will never gain any sympathy from the other party; no, sometimes you won't even get a reaction because here, it's entirely a sphere of influence of gold, and with your poor appearance, you can't even dream of stepping in! This is the truth, I'm not lying to you.

[However, don't be discouraged, and don't be sad. As long as you can seize the gold, you can satisfy everything. The problem of a single woman is really small! There are so many women in the world, beautiful women are snatched away by rich people one by one, and if they're sad, they will be replenished batch after batch to adapt to the needs of this era. Therefore, at this moment, don't pursue women, you should pursue gold first. Once the money in your pocket is full, then, regardless of whether your beard is already long, there will naturally be peerless young beauties to serve you with gentleness and consideration. Don't say one, you can have ten or eight, as long as you are happy, you won't have to worry about scarcity. Even if she is a first-class celebrity, as long as you have money, you can always buy her!

[Friend, are you pursuing too? Do you also feel sexual frustration? If you ask yourself if you have all the requirements for romance, and you don't, then I am willing to give you a piece of advice: let's first think of a way to make money!]

Seaside Jottings 194

— Ci Min

丨What I Saw After the Calamity丨

A light breeze brushes by, the seawater ripples slightly, on a grassy ground, several cloth tents are pitched, a gramophone releases melodious and soft tunes, intoxicating pairs of modern men and women dozing side by side, pear skins, chestnut shells, and empty bottles of whiskey and soda water are strewn all around them like mud figures who have drunk themselves senseless!

The two cannons that were blasted to pieces by enemy warships during the Shanghai battle still lie in the withered yellow autumn grass, unattended. But the spiral nails all over their bodies have long been stolen and sold by people. When I went up to take a closer look, the words "[Made by the Jiangnan Manufacturing Bureau in the 27th year of Guangxu]" clearly leapt into my eyes. Ah! Blue-eyed devils, Japanese, often pass by here, I wonder what they think when they see it?

Several yellow oxen, with their heads lowered, wag their tails as they graze contentedly, they seem to have forgotten the rope that people have tied in their nostrils! Farmers hold scythes, diligently and steadily, some are harvesting sorghum, some are cutting down rice stalks, they simply don't think about how deep the sea is in front of them, or how high the sky is above them. Swallows, reluctant to leave their homeland, soar over the clear and pure sea, not heading south.

Our country's sailing ships, British merchant ships, and Japanese warships, in the setting sun of dusk, are heading towards their respective destinations!

The Hair of Female Workers in Silk and紗 Factories 195

— Ms. Pu Wuxiu

It is Inappropriate to Cut it Off; All Should Wear Buns

Women wearing their hair long has been a long-standing custom, and elegance arises from cloud-like hair and misty temples. Indeed, women cherish their hair as if it were their second life. However, as times change and the world shifts, the trend of cutting hair has become popular. Young ladies from humble families and daughters from wealthy households, seeking beautification, all find it quick to cut their hair. Occasionally, due to the prohibition of fathers and brothers, or the disapproval of husbands, some still have to wear a long braid or a low bun, but these are only a minority. Female workers in纱 and silk factories, with long, dangling black braids, get their braids caught in the belts due to the wind, and as a result, dozens lose their lives every year. For example, A-mei, a female worker from Changzhou in the fine yarn section of the Yong'an纱 Factory in Wusong Yuncaobang, as reported in the Ten-Day News, is one such case. The report stated that A-mei, while working on the morning of the ninth, inadvertently had her braid caught in the belt, and in an instant, the long braid was pulled away with the scalp, causing injury and leaving her life in danger. Seeing this, it seems that female workers should cut their hair to ensure safety.

However, in all things under heaven, there are benefits and drawbacks. The local silk factories previously received a cable from European manufacturers, stating that while Chinese silk is of excellent quality, it is occasionally mixed with short hair. If artificial methods are used to remove it, it would be extremely laborious. If scientific methods are used to eliminate it, it is feared that it would damage the silk warp. The best way to handle this matter is to inform the female workers not to cut their hair while working. In fact, when the motor is turned on and the belt is rotating, the wind force is quite strong, and the short hair of female workers who have cut their hair often blows down and mixes into the silk, making it difficult to sell abroad.

In my opinion, if female workers can avoid wearing braids and cutting their hair, and all wear buns, then even if hair falls out from the roots, due to being tied tightly, it won't fall down unless untied and re-tied. In this way, both parties can be taken care of and both can benefit. It is safe during work, and the product is clean and unmixed. It will be seen that it will become popular globally and sell well everywhere, then inferior Japanese goods will naturally have no place to be used. I hope that those in charge of each factory will not neglect it because it is minor. (Moved to donate to the Northeast Volunteer Army)

Entering the Pass, Postal Partners (19) 196

— Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

It turned out that佟一貞's uncle, 佟貴福, was originally a member of the Eight Banners, and his mind was so old and rotten that he always blamed the Manchu people for losing the country and the absence of the True Dragon Emperor for his own poor situation, which prevented him from enjoying the imperial favor again. Now, hearing that 宣統 had ascended the throne in Changchun and restored the Manchukuo, he thought that he had another good opportunity to serve the dragon, and it would not be difficult to rise to prominence and still be among the ranks of the nobles. However, he did not know that 溥儀 was just a leader of prisoners, a puppet manipulated by the Japanese. Where in the world was there a real Manchukuo? He was just having such a dream in vain, and he still had to be loyal and look down on 魯伯勤. He was really a big fool in the world.

魯伯勤 was young and vigorous, and he wanted to argue with 佟貴福, who was so deranged and stubborn, or at least give him some warnings. But considering 佟一貞's sake, he didn't want to harm the thing he valued because of the rat nearby, and he couldn't let him lose his temper at will; and 佟一貞 was also painstakingly mediating in secret, repeatedly advising him not to take this stubborn man's words seriously, it was best to ignore him, and he had to reluctantly learn to pretend to be deaf and dumb and laugh it off. It's just that they didn't see eye to eye, so from then on, he became too lazy to go to 佟's house, preferring to still meet 佟一貞 in the open air, and no longer look at 佟貴福's strange face that was tasteless in speech and hateful in appearance.

Unexpectedly, unpleasant things came one after another. The post office, where 魯伯勒 had entrusted his life, also gradually had many unfortunate entanglements, and there was a danger of shaking and collapsing. As his cousin had predicted before, the Japanese methods were extremely vicious, and they had to completely erode all the rights and interests of the Northeast. They would never allow the only remaining post office of the Republic of China to continue to exercise its powers safely. At this time, unfortunately, the prediction came true.

The process of this change was as follows: at first, the Japanese used the excuse of inspecting books, newspapers, and letters sent from various places within the pass, and sent some inspectors to the post office to randomly tear open the mail, flailing their hands and feet, and rushing around. The arrogance was really great. They also suspected that the post office staff secretly released the Tianjin-Hankou newspapers, preventing them from detaining them, and often became angry and said they wanted to execute people, and they had already quarreled with the post office staff. Recently, using Manchukuo as a cover, they actually wanted to transfer the entire postal service of the three northeastern provinces to Manchukuo, and limited the postmaster to set a date for the handover. They also threatened the general postal staff in every way, requiring them to continue to serve Manchukuo faithfully, otherwise they would send a military police team to arrest them. Although the postmaster was fortunately a European and American, he still dared to find foreign consuls to argue with them, but when they argued to the point of exhaustion, they still could not match the barbaric force. It was clear that this only surviving post office of the Republic of China could not be protected! Relying on the postmaster's protection, the staff may still be able to obtain a passport to leave the country, but can they really be sent away so cheaply? In the end, no one dared to guarantee it.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Iron Statue 214

— Buddha

The newspaper reported the other day that someone suggested abolishing the Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance and proposed casting iron statues for those who advocated civil war, placing them in important locations in this city, so as to serve as a warning. I don't really agree with this method of punishment because this kind of honorary punishment is not only outdated, but also not sufficient to be effective.

"People above three generations are afraid of good names; people below three generations are afraid of not having good names." Generally speaking, people in the past still valued integrity and virtue, so they cast iron statues of traitors like Qin Hui to warn everyone not to commit similar crimes. But the warlords of today only have power and territory in their eyes. They will not be deterred by your iron statues. As the saying goes, "Let them laugh and scold; I'll still be a good official." So, such a method was also used during the old warlord era. But what effect did it have?

The people oppose civil war and organize groups to oppose it. This has been stated repeatedly and emphatically. Suppose they still have some sense of the people in their minds, they definitely won't start another civil war. Suppose they still have the whole country in their minds, they also definitely won't dare to start another civil war given the deep and great external troubles before our eyes. Because they don't put the people and the country in their hearts at all, so external troubles are just external troubles, and civil war is just civil war. What else is there to say?

"If you can't leave a fragrant name for a hundred generations, why not leave a stinking name for ten thousand years?" This was originally a saying of the ancients. Because it's not easy to leave a fragrant name for a hundred generations, and it's not easy to leave a stinking name for ten thousand years. Therefore, casting iron statues for them is tantamount to promoting them. I'm afraid they'd even seek it and not get it. Moreover, in the past, there were only a few powerful and treacherous people like Qin Hui and Zhang Jun, so it was easy to cast iron statues. Now, it's not easy to understand the rights and wrongs of the two sides in the civil war. Should only the civil war leaders of one side be cast? Or should the civil war leaders of both sides be cast? There's also the fact that the current leaders of the civil war may not just be these few leaders. I'm afraid there are also many people behind the scenes. And the people behind the scenes are even more ruthless than those in front. So, should only the leaders in front be cast? | It wouldn't be fair |. If the leaders behind the scenes are all cast in it, not only would it be impossible to cast them all, but there would also be no evidence. Where would we even start?

Therefore, I don't advocate casting iron statues. Casting iron statues is completely a meaningless act. So, if we want to actively advocate the abolition of civil war, we should think of stronger and more effective methods. Otherwise, we can only listen to their civil war. They commit suicide and everyone goes down together one day.

Science

Artificial Pigments of Yellow, Blue, and Green 217

— Shen Erming

Artificial red and white pigments have already been published in previous issues of this journal, but other colors have not been mentioned, so I will select the simple and common ones to introduce below:

Artificial Yellow Pigments

Mosaic Gold SnS2 Method: Use 40 parts of tin powder, 35 parts of sulfur, and 25 parts of quicksand, or 80 parts of tetravalent tin oxide, 60 parts of sulfur, and 30 parts of saltpeter, or 20 parts of divalent tin sulfide, 10 parts of sulfur, and 8 parts of sal ammoniac. Place in an iron pot and heat to dark red to obtain golden tetravalent tin sulfide. If the temperature exceeds 650 degrees Celsius, this substance will thermally decompose into divalent tin sulfide. The iron pot has a lid and a gooseneck tube connecting to a condenser. The sal ammoniac is recovered here and can be reused. Mosaic gold and glue can be used as gold paint.

Yellow Lead Oxide Pbo Method: Place lead in a rotating furnace and oxidize it with air blown by a fan. The yellow lead oxide produced by the indigenous method of using saltpeter as an oxidizing agent in China is not durable and easily hardens and becomes useless. It dries easily with oil, so it is a drying agent. Yellow lead oxide is also used as a raw material for glass and porcelain enamel.

Barium Yellow BaCro4 Method: Add a barium chloride solution to a sodium dichromate solution. The resulting yellow precipitate is barium yellow. Its coloring power is not strong, but it is stable and durable. It is used in oil paints and watercolors.

Zinc Yellow ZnCro4 Method: Add potassium chromate to a neutralized hot solution of zinc sulfate, or boil 10 parts of potassium dichromate with 75 parts of zinc white. The resulting precipitate is zinc yellow. Zinc yellow is soluble in water, so it is not suitable for external use. Its covering power and coloring power are weak, but its color is very good. It is used to prevent rust on steel, but protective varnish must be applied.

Lead Yellow PdCro4 Method: Mix 40 parts of lead acetate in 160 parts of water to make solution A, and dissolve 31 parts of sodium dichromate in the same amount of water to make solution B. Mix solutions A and B to produce a precipitate. Filter and dry it. Alternatively, dissolve 100 pounds of lead nitrate in 600 pounds of water at 50 degrees Fahrenheit to make solution A, and dissolve 35 pounds of sodium dichromate in the same temperature and quantity of water to make solution B. Place 2,000 pounds of water at 50 degrees Fahrenheit in a precipitation tank, inject solutions A and B simultaneously and mix thoroughly, allow it to settle, filter, wash the precipitate thoroughly, heat to 180 degrees Fahrenheit and dry it. It is even better to use a vacuum drying method.

Page 17

Cadmium Yellow Cds Method: Combine salt solutions containing Cc and S ions to obtain a precipitate. Cadmium yellow is used in painting inks.

Artificial Green Pigments

Chrome Green Cr2o(Oh)4 Method: Mix three parts of boric acid and eight parts of potassium dichromate with water to form a paste. Heat in a reverberatory furnace for four hours to obtain a porous substance called chrome borate. Pour into cold water to obtain chrome green. Chrome green is stable and resistant to alkali, light, and heat. It is used in automobile canopy paint, engine paint, wall paint, etc.

Arsenic Green Method: Mix four parts of sodium carbonate in 20 parts of water and dissolve three parts of trivalent arsenic oxide to make solution A. Mix three parts of copper sulfate (blue vitriol) in 40 parts of water to make solution B. Mix the two solutions to produce a precipitate. Filter to obtain arsenic green. Arsenic green is poisonous and has excellent color. It is used in artwork. If it is ground with oil for too long, the color will darken. However, it is durable in seawater, which is its advantage.

Copper Green Cu2(Oh)2Co3 Method: Add a sodium carbonate solution to blue vitriol solution to obtain a precipitate. Copper green is light-resistant, but its covering power is weak. It is used in painting inks.

Lead Green Method: Dissolve 27 to 28 parts of lead acetate and 3 to 4 parts of ferrous sulfate separately in water. Dissolve 3 to 4 parts of potassium ferrocyanide and 9 parts of sodium dichromate in the same container with water. Place water and 200 parts of heavy chalk powder in a precipitation tank. Inject all three solutions simultaneously while mixing and filtering. Dry the precipitate. Lead green is used in oil paints and inks. However, lead green is not suitable for oil paints in seaside air containing salt.

Zinc Green It is a mixture of zinc yellow and ultramarine blue. The manufacturing method is similar to lead green. It is suitable for interior decoration. Because it often spreads when exposed to water, it is often used in car paint, but protective varnish must be added to protect it.

Artificial Blue Pigments

Ultramarine Blue 2(Kfefe(Cn)6)3.5H2O Method: Dissolve 20 parts of ferrous sulfate in 300 parts of water to make solution A. Dissolve 20 parts of potassium ferrocyanide and add 1 part of hydrochloric acid in 600 parts of water to make solution B. Mix both solutions thoroughly, add 8 parts of bleaching powder, and promote oxidation with direct steam. Allow to settle, filter, and wash the precipitate multiple times in the filter. Dry it. Ultramarine blue has rich coloring power and is used in oil paints, inks, and leather paint.

Blue Lead The composition is very complex. It is obtained by sublimation of galena. It is not affected by sulfur-containing gases. It is used for protective paint for steel.

Ultramarine The chemical formula for less sandy ultramarine is 4Na2Al2Si2o8 + Na2S4, and for more sandy ultramarine, it is 2Na2Al2Si3Oio + Na2S4. There are two manufacturing methods:

(1) Sodium Sulfate Method: Use porcelain clay, sodium sulfate, carbon, sulfur, and sand as raw materials. Grind finely and place in a muffle furnace without contact with air. Heat to bright red for 8 hours to obtain a dark green porous body. Grind finely and spread in a shallow cloth tray about an inch thick. Cover with sulfur powder and heat to obtain a blue substance. Grind finely and wash with water to remove sodium sulfate and sodium sulfite. Boil with sodium sulfide solution to remove sulfur.

(2) Sodium Carbonate Method: Use porcelain clay, sodium carbonate, carbon, sulfur, and sand as raw materials. Grind finely and spread in a muffle furnace to a thickness of 14 inches. Heat for 3 to 4 weeks, and cool for 10 to 12 days. The resulting substance is blue on the top and greenish on the bottom. Separate and levigate with water. Ultramarine is heat-resistant and alkali-resistant and is used in wall paint and car paint. Lead-containing objects cannot be used together.

Improve Social Discussion Meeting

The Rickshaw Problem 218

— Hui

In Japan, the place where rickshaws originated, they have gradually become rare and uncommon. This is because they know that pulling a rickshaw is inhumane and goes against human dignity, something that should not exist in the world. However, in our China, it is still thriving. Today one company [Li Yun], tomorrow another [Da Sheng]. Rickshaw companies are constantly increasing and developing. The old use them to exploit, the pullers risk their lives to survive, and passengers rely on them as a convenient means of transportation.

Just taking Shanghai as an example, if we stand on an ordinary street and pay attention, it probably won't take a minute before at least ten rickshaws pass by. As for the bustling downtown areas, of course, they are constantly passing by. There are so many people who make a living by pulling rickshaws! Someone asks: [How can there be so many people in Shanghai pulling rickshaws?] The fact tells you: [They are not locals. They abandoned their homes, gardens, fields, land, hoes, plows, stone mills, water mortars, cattle, chickens... and ran to Shanghai to suffer and struggle?] But why did they abandon everything they had! The answer is very simple: [Bandits, disasters, high interest rates, heavy taxes: and the expansion of capitalist forces into the countryside... The countryside thus collapsed unconditionally, and everything they had was destroyed! So one by one, they came to the cities. What can the cities give them to do? Inevitably, they became slaves of the capitalists.

[Labor is sacred], can this be applied to the coolies who make a living by pulling rickshaws? This is simply a deceitful and numbing phrase for the suffering and weak! Some people think that rickshaw pullers earn one or two dollars a day, which accumulates over time and is quite considerable. If hard work is compensated, that would be fine. In fact, even ten times that amount cannot compensate for one ten-thousandth of what they sacrifice! Because they (1) overwork; (2) are malnourished; (3) lack sleep; (4) live in terrible conditions... Of course, their health is destroyed! What remains, if you look, are just yellow faces, skinny bones, hunched waists, crooked backs, and two legs moving!

Some people have also realized that pulling a rickshaw is not a human

Page 18

life, it is cruel and inhumane. However, they only [realize it], and at most they passively do not ride. Sometimes, because of urgency or distance, they have to rely on it to walk. At this time, if the rickshaw puller runs a little slower, they forget about [humanity] [ghostly morality], and they will definitely kick the footrest [Pig! Faster!] Or if the rickshaw puller argues about the price, they will quickly repay them with their mouths, humming [bastard!]... Or some people think [in Shanghai, where merchants gather and material civilization prospers, rickshaws should not be kept, because this damages China's international dignity and causes foreigners to laugh at our cultural backwardness, so they should be unconditionally expelled like prostitutes in Luoyang...] These, these, like this, like that, is this considered [humanity]? Is this considered sympathy? Or is this considered a complete solution to the rickshaw problem? Get out of here!

Now, we plead for the rickshaw pullers, asking the capitalists themselves to realize that [humans eating humans will only lead to everyone's destruction and ruin]! What's the point? Secondly, let us join hands and work together to re-evaluate and rebuild an ideal new life, a new society! Let us first take these two paths:

(1) Because they come from the countryside, the countryside should be scientifically constructed, the rural economy should be consolidated, rural education should be developed; and large-scale, planned reclamation groups should be organized, focusing on production and development.

(2) Because they have no work, the rich should abandon their consistent policy of exploiting others for their own benefit, and put aside their traditional speculative and adventurous businesses. Please gather strong capital.

Establish many large-scale, scientifically managed factories, focusing on production and construction.

Finally, I shout again: [The rickshaw problem is not a local, individual problem, it is a whole social problem!]

Generous

Why Not? 219

— Iron Blood Man

[It's been several years since I last saw your friends, Mr. L. Since the Shanghai War, they've moved to a new house on M Road in a certain concession!] My sister said to me.

[Of course: life is important! Do they not want their lives! And they are now a family with the added character of "rich"! ] I replied while flipping through the newspaper.

[But...] A command suddenly came from my heart; I had to pay them a visit. So I put down the newspaper, immediately put on a long gown that was neither too long nor too short, and ran out the door. It was only eight o'clock, and after running for about half an hour, I finally found the new house. Suddenly, I heard a sharp voice, as if scolding me! I turned around and looked, ah! It turned out to be Miss S, Mr. C's sister.

[We live in this house, please come in and have a seat, my brother just went out!] She said to me with a face smiling like a Buddha.

[Ah! Mr. C, it's been a long time!] Her mother said with a smile.

[It's been a long time; since the Shanghai War, have you suffered any losses?] I asked.

[We didn't suffer any losses, anyway...] [She was interrupted].

[Mom! Brother is back], Miss S ran over and shouted like a flying arrow.

[What wind blew you here, Mr. Jun? It's been many years since I've seen you,] Mr. L said somewhat coldly, with a hint of pride.

Later, we chatted about this and that, and after talking for a while, [have some snacks], he took out some snacks and asked me to eat them. I was honest and didn't hold back, eating a lot, not caring about anything;

[Alas! Today was extremely "unlucky"!] He said with a sigh.

[What "unlucky"? You might as well tell me], I asked suspiciously.

Because she [Mr. L's lover] promised me yesterday that she would definitely go with me to the salon tomorrow to get a manicure. This morning, we both ran to our destination. In less than half an hour, she got it done and paid a dollar to that woman [the Western woman who does manicures]. Later, I also took out a dollar to get a manicure, but she accidentally made my finger bleed, which really hurt me a lot. I knew that for the price of one dollar, I would get [pain]. Aren't you angry], he shouted through gritted teeth.

Hearing these words almost choked me to death; I had just taken a bite of cake, which was stuck in my throat, neither up nor down, and I used all my sucking power to swallow it.

[Think about it, someone like you is really stupid. If you had donated that dollar to the Northeastern Volunteer Army, you could have bought a few bullets and killed the "dwarves" [Japanese] to your heart's content! "Why not?" ] (A suitable ending)

The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Wang Youqing, having received stolen goods, is sentenced to thirty days of detention. The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day.

Judgment in the Chen Jinyong Robbery Case (Main Text): 231

Chen Jinyong, having snatched the property of others, is sentenced to four months imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

Judgment in the Wang Zhimei Opium Case (Main Text): 232

Wang Zhimei, having assisted in possessing opium substitutes with intent to sell, is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it can be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Two catties and two ounces of the opium substitute red pills are confiscated and burned.

Judgment in the Cai Arong Theft Case (Main Text): 233

Cai Arong, having repeatedly committed theft, is sentenced to six months imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

Judgment in the Xia Ruyu et al. Case of Disrupting a Family (Main Text): 234

Xia Ruyu, with the intention of profit, enticed a man under the age of twenty and is sentenced to two years imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention are converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Wang Zhihan and Xia Chenshi are found not guilty. The trial for Gu Xiaoliuzi is suspended.

Civil Judgments:

Judgment in the Shunjiu Mark et al. versus Dingchang Rice Shop Lawsuit regarding Rice Payment (Main Text): 235

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff Shunjiu Mark rice payment of six hundred and eighty-eight yuan, six jiao, and eight fen; and shall repay the plaintiff Yiyuanxing Mark rice payment of six hundred and seven yuan, three jiao. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Judgment in the Longhua Company versus Yao Songnian Appeal regarding Rice Payment (Main Text): 236

The appeal is dismissed. The second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

Judgment in the Xinchang Leather Factory versus Shengshengchang Shoe Store Lawsuit regarding Loans (Main Text): 237

The defendant shall repay the plaintiff a loan of one hundred and thirty-nine yuan and eight jiao and six fen. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Judgment in the Yang Yunlong versus Dai Zhaofeng et al. Lawsuit regarding Rent Arrears (Main Text): 238

The defendant Dai Zhaofeng shall pay the plaintiff rent of two hundred and forty-two yuan. If unable to pay, Wang Rongxin shall be responsible for paying on his behalf. Litigation costs shall be borne by Dai Zhaofeng.

Public Notice of Service:

Judgment in the Wu Defu versus Chen Putian Lawsuit regarding Rent Arrears (Main Text): 239

The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of five hundred and forty-six yuan and vacate the premises. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. Notice is hereby given to the defendant Chen Putian.

Li Yinian versus Chen Ziyi Lawsuit regarding Rent Arrears: 240

This court has scheduled a public hearing for 9:00 AM on November 12th. The defendant is hereby notified to appear in court for debate on time and must not delay on their own. This is a public notice of service to the defendant Chen Ziyi.

▲Huang Jiefu's application for execution: We have read the petition and will summon the case for questioning and pursuing. This instruction.

▲Zhao Zhushi's application for execution: We have read the petition and will summon the case for questioning and pursuing. This instruction.

▲Deng Yuanhe's application to recall the square receipt from the creditor for collection: We have read the petition and will summon the creditor for questioning and decision. This instruction.

▲Zhang Shenshi's application for execution: We have read the petition and will summon for questioning and pursuing. This instruction.

▲Fang Chaozong's continued petition for execution: We have read the petition and will summon the case for strict pursuit. This instruction.

▲Hu Shangsheng's application to return the execution to this court: We have read the petition and will summon the case for questioning and pursuing. This instruction.

▲Zhu Panshi's request for deferred payment: We have read the petition and temporarily allow the money to be paid in full within ten days. The request for installment payments should not be discussed. This instruction.

▲Shen Qiangren's petition to extend the payment deadline: We have read the petition and approve extending the deadline by ten days. The money must be paid to the case, and pursuit will be made to the guarantor if the deadline is exceeded, without error. This instruction.

▲Tao Yiqing's petition to request exemption from execution: We have read the petition and order that you invite the creditor to come to court in person to declare, and there must be no evasion. This instruction.

▲Hu Zhongyu's request to extend the payment deadline for the Feng Binggui debt settlement case: We have read the petition and order that you quickly raise the outstanding debt within one week and pay it into the case, without further delay. This instruction.

▲Mo Xinyi's request for execution for the Zhang Deting rental case: We have read the petition and will summon the case for questioning and pursuing. This instruction.

▲Wu Defu's request for exemption from execution for the Sen Yitai et al. rental case: We have read the petition. Sen Yitai has already paid part of the rent, and the remaining payment is scheduled for payment. Lu Baolin has requested exemption from pursuit for the rent outside of Chuchu. File for record. This instruction.

▲Wang Renyu's request for the cancellation of the provisional attachment and the unsealing and return of the property for the Wang Tingxuan repayment settlement case: We have read the petition and approve the cancellation of the provisional attachment and will dispatch personnel to unseal and return the property for collection. This instruction.

▲Li Yongtang's request for the prompt arrest and rigorous pursuit of the Wu Zhongtang bill case: We have read the petition and have already rigorously executed it. This instruction.

▲Cheng Guiting's application for execution for the Ji Shenshi pawn case: We have read the petition, but the case is not yet decided, so the request should be considered later. This instruction.

▲Bao Jiashan's petition to move and store sealed items: We have read the petition and order that you designate an appropriate house and report it to this court, and we will dispatch personnel to supervise the move and sealing. This instruction.

Civil Instructions:

▲San You Industrial Cooperative's request to copy documents from the case file: We have read the petition. The case file has already been submitted to the Jiangsu Higher Court, so you should apply to the Higher Court for copying. This instruction.

▲Xie Jinyuan's application for registration of expulsion of an unruly son: We have read the petition. The request has no legal basis and cannot be approved. This instruction.

▲Lu Daosan's application for registration that his apprentice has run away and cannot be found: We have read the petition. It is impossible to guess the truth of the alleged details, so the request for registration cannot be approved. This instruction.

Instructions:

▲Wang Qihong sues Yang Dianxun and Wang Chenshi et al. for disrupting marriage: We have read the petition. If the defendants do have illegal behavior, you should report it to the police and send it to the case for review and processing. This instruction.

▲Le Huan's request for investigation because her daughter-in-law has run away: We have read the petition. The elopement of your daughter-in-law is not the fault of anyone, so the request is denied. This instruction.

▲Cui Qingsong sues Li Shuanglin for fornication: We have read the petition. The citizen has no right to interfere with his concubine's affair with another person, so the request is denied. This instruction.

▲Lin Delong sues Xiang Xianchang et al. for withholding vehicle reports: We have read the petition. Whether Xu Wenbin et al. withhold the vehicle reports for legitimate reasons or whether it is a dispute over business operations is a civil dispute and should be submitted to the Civil Court for review and processing. You should be informed of this. This instruction.

▲Huang Xiaodangzi sues Xu Ziqing et al. for seduction: We have read the petition. If Xu Ziqing et al. have committed seduction, you can report it to the police station at any time and bring the case to justice. You should be informed of this. This instruction.

▲Wang Keyang sues Zhang Zhixiang for fraud: We have read the petition. Zhang Zhixiang et al.'s breach of contract and refusal to perform is purely a civil dispute, and the request to summon for investigation cannot be approved. This instruction.

▲Huang Anyin sues Yan Zhusan for fraud: We have read the petition. If Yan has requested money and has been taken to the police station by the patrol police, why was it only reprimanded? The lawsuit is obviously untrue and cannot be approved for questioning. This instruction.

▲Lu Jingao sues Li Guanwen for injury: We have read the petition and order that you come to the court for questioning. This instruction.

▲Cai Jingan and Tong Zhao sue Cai Wushi for theft: We have read the petition. Since you know the whereabouts of the defendant, if the lawsuit is true, you can twist them to the police station and send them to the court for review and processing. This instruction.

▲Zhang Changyuan's petition for registration: We have read the petition. The current Code of Criminal Procedure does not have any explicit regulations for registration, so the request should not be discussed. This instruction.

▲Zhu Jiuxiang's petition to transfer the document for proposal: We have read the petition and will send a letter to the Nanjing Municipal Public Security Bureau for further review and processing. This instruction.

▲Shi Xinqi's petition to guarantee Chen Longjiang: We have read the petition. The residence of this person is not within the jurisdiction of this court, so the request should not be discussed. This instruction.

▲Gao Jiru sues Hong Feng for extortion: We have read the petition. Someone came to inquire because their younger brother was missing, so why is it referred to as extortion? The request is denied. This instruction.

▲Zheng Zhidong sues Sun, a patrol officer, for extortion of illegal fees: We have read the petition. Since this person was detained for robbery, they should be dealt with by the Public Security Bureau according to the law. The request to welcome and bring them in is difficult to approve. This instruction.

▲Chen Jinkui sues Chen Wangshi for adultery: We have read the petition. Your wife's previous crime of adultery has already been pardoned and will not be investigated further. If she has recently had an affair with someone, you are allowed to report it to the police station and bring the case for review and processing. You should be informed of this. This instruction.

▲Zhou Yonglin sues Tong et al. for adultery and occupation: We have read the petition. Since your sister is married, you have no right to interfere whether she has been sexually violated, so the request is denied. This instruction.

▲Hai Men Yuan Pinzhen requests the return of the case file: We have read the petition. The case has been transferred to the jurisdiction of this court, and the case file should be kept by this court and should not be returned to the original county. You should be informed of this. This instruction.

▲Jin Liushi sues Jin Shanfu for abandonment: We have read the petition. Since this person is only twenty-two years old and capable of supporting themself, there is no issue of abandonment, so the request is denied. This instruction.

▲Yan Jinsheng et al. petition to withdraw the complaint: We have read the petition and approve the withdrawal of the complaint. This instruction.

▲Wang Kaihe sues Wang Wushi, Dong Lianjin et al. for disrupting marriage: We have read the petition. If the defendants do have enticement, you should report it to the police and send it to the case for review and processing. This instruction.

▲Zhu Jialu sues Wang Weiqing et al. for disrupting marriage: We have read the petition and can release without further questioning. You should be informed of this. This instruction. (The above are from October 20th)
